//***************************************************************************
//*
//*  Custom Script Code
//*
//***************************************************************************

//***************************************************************************
//*
//*  Map Item Tables
//*
//***************************************************************************

function ItemTable000000_DropItems takes nothing returns nothing
    local widget trigWidget= null
    local unit trigUnit= null
    local integer itemID= 0
    local boolean canDrop= true

    set trigWidget=bj_lastDyingWidget
    if ( trigWidget == null ) then
        set trigUnit=GetTriggerUnit()
    endif

    if ( trigUnit != null ) then
        set canDrop=not IsUnitHidden(trigUnit)
        if ( canDrop and GetChangingUnit() != null ) then
            set canDrop=( GetChangingUnitPrevOwner() == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) )
        endif
    endif

    if ( canDrop ) then
        // Item set 0
        call RandomDistReset()
        call RandomDistAddItem(ChooseRandomItemEx(ITEM_TYPE_CHARGED, 2), 30)
        call RandomDistAddItem(ChooseRandomItemEx(ITEM_TYPE_POWERUP, 1), 20)
        call RandomDistAddItem(- 1, 50)
        set itemID=RandomDistChoose()
        if ( trigUnit != null ) then
            call UnitDropItem(trigUnit, itemID)
        else
            call WidgetDropItem(trigWidget, itemID)
        endif

    endif

    set bj_lastDyingWidget=null
    call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

    call CreateUnitsForPlayer11()
endfunction

    call CreateNeutralHostileBuildings()
    call CreateNeutralPassiveBuildings()
    call CreatePlayerBuildings()
    call CreateNeutralHostile()
    call CreateNeutralPassive()
    call CreatePlayerUnits()
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Initialization
//
// Setup for: weather, random terrain, teams, players, AI, team colors and starting doodad animations.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ZTg3' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LTr2' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'BTrx' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LOcg' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ZTg1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITx1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITig' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITf2' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'BTrs' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITf3' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'NTbd' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ZTg4' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITf1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'IOt1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT04' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT15' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ZTr2' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ZTr0' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITf4' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT15' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT06' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Func020A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001C() ) then
        call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), "death")
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func020Func001Func001C() ) then
            call SetDestructableInvulnerableBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), true)
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Func042A takes nothing returns nothing

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Initialization_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Time and Animations
    call SetTimeOfDay(6.01)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LOtz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LOlp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LObz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'NOfp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'CPct', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("Stand Upgrade First", 'YS07', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("Stand Upgrade Second", 'LSgs', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(gg_dest_LTex_5975, "death")
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSin', gg_rct_Forest_2)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand work", 'LSba', gg_rct_Moladune)
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(gg_unit_nbot_0466, true)
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(gg_unit_nbot_0392, true)
    call KillDestructable(gg_dest_LTt5_3413)
    call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_ITg4_0345)
    call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_LTe2_4003)
    set udg_DwarfGateOpen=true
    set udg_ForestGateOpen=true
    call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect(), function Trig_Initialization_Func020A)
    // Variable Setup
    set udg_PlayerColor[1]="|CFFFF0000"
    set udg_PlayerColor[2]="|CFF0000FF"
    set udg_PlayerColor[3]="|CFF18E7BD"
    set udg_PlayerColor[4]="|CFF520084"
    set udg_PlayerColor[5]="|CFFFFFF00"
    set udg_PlayerColor[6]="|CFFFF8A08"
    set udg_PlayerColor[7]="|CFF18BE00"
    set udg_PlayerColor[8]="|CFFE759AD"
    set udg_SpecialZombie[1]='u000'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[2]='n00A'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[3]='n00B'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[4]='u002'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[5]='u008'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[6]='n00G'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[7]='u001'
    set udg_SpecialZombie[8]='n000'
    call InitHashtableBJ()
    set udg_FireHashtable=GetLastCreatedHashtableBJ()
    call SetAltMinimapIcon("UI\\Minimap\\MiniMap-Entrance.blp")
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('nzin')
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Initialization_Func042A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    // Player Setup
    set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=8
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func045Func001C() ) then
            call ForceAddPlayerSimple(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()), udg_NeutralPlayers)
            set udg_PlayerCount=( udg_PlayerCount + 1 )
            set udg_HeroSummons[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(1000, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
            call SetPlayerFlagBJ(PLAYER_STATE_GIVES_BOUNTY, true, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()))
            call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('h009', 1, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()))
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A031', ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()))
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A032', ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()))
            call CreateFogModifierRectBJ(true, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()), FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, GetPlayableMapRect())
            call FogModifierStart(GetLastCreatedFogModifier())
            call DestroyFogModifier(GetLastCreatedFogModifier())
        else
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()))
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Initialization_Func045Func001Func002A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        endif
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers, udg_NeutralPlayers, bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
    set udg_SpecialLimit=( 40 - ( CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers) * 2 ) )
    set udg_SpecialCount=CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers)
    call SetAllyColorFilterState(0)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func050C() ) then
        set udg_Hardmode=true
    else
    endif
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=9
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerColorBJ(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), GetPlayerColor(Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE)), true)
        call SetPlayerOnScoreScreenBJ(false, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()))
        call SetPlayerFlagBJ(PLAYER_STATE_GIVES_BOUNTY, true, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()))
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Shipyard)
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(gg_unit_h00L_0708, "patrol", udg_TempLoc)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('u00B')
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Initialization_Func056A)
     call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    // Animal Spawn Points
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect())
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Initialization_Func061A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    // Game Difficulty and AI
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 5)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func065C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_1)
        set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_4)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func065Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_2)
            set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_3)
        else
            if ( Trig_Initialization_Func065Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_5)
                set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_1)
            else
                if ( Trig_Initialization_Func065Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_4)
                    set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_2)
                else
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_3)
                    set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Graveyard_5)
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'U007', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_Necromancer=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call SetHeroLevelBJ(udg_Necromancer, CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers), false)
    set udg_DeathPoint=GetUnitLoc(udg_Necromancer)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func070C() ) then
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('spsh', udg_Necromancer)
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('lnrn', udg_Necromancer)
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(7, ITEM_TYPE_CAMPAIGN), udg_Necromancer)
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(7, ITEM_TYPE_ARTIFACT), udg_Necromancer)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func070Func002C() ) then
            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('spsh', udg_Necromancer)
            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rnsp', udg_Necromancer)
            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(6, ITEM_TYPE_CAMPAIGN), udg_Necromancer)
        else
            if ( Trig_Initialization_Func070Func002Func002C() ) then
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('spsh', udg_Necromancer)
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rlif', udg_Necromancer)
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func071C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('Rume', 2, Player(11))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('Ruar', 2, Player(11))
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func071Func005C() ) then
            call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('Rume', 1, Player(11))
            call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('Ruar', 1, Player(11))
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        else
            if ( Trig_Initialization_Func071Func005Func003C() ) then
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            else
                if ( Trig_Initialization_Func071Func005Func003Func001C() ) then
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u000', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                else
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    set udg_ZombieGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(Player(11))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_ZombieGroup, function Trig_Initialization_Func075A)
    call ForceAddPlayerSimple(Player(8), udg_Townsfolk)
    call ForceAddPlayerSimple(Player(9), udg_Townsfolk)
    call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers, udg_Townsfolk, bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
    call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_Townsfolk, udg_NeutralPlayers, bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
    call StartCampaignAI(Player(9), "war3mapImported\\Townsfolk.ai")
    call RemoveAllGuardPositions(Player(11))
    // Weather Effects
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Lowlands, 'FDwh')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[0]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Lowlands, 'RAhr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[1]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Lowlands, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[2]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 3
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Highlands, 'WOlw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[3]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Highlands, 'RAhr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[4]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Highlands, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[5]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 6
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_North_Badlands, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[6]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_North_Badlands, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[7]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_North_Badlands, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[8]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 9
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_1, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[9]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_1, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[10]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_1, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[11]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 12
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_2, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[12]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_2, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[13]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_West_Badlands_2, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[14]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 15
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Stone_Path, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[15]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Stone_Path, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[16]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Stone_Path, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[17]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 18
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_1, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[18]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_1, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[19]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_1, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[20]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 21
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_2, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[21]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_2, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[22]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Spire_Flats_2, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[23]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // 24
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Discover_Raiders_Outpost, 'WOcw')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[24]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Discover_Raiders_Outpost, 'RAlr')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[25]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    call AddWeatherEffectSaveLast(gg_rct_Discover_Raiders_Outpost, 'LRaa')
    set udg_Weather_Effects[26]=GetLastCreatedWeatherEffect()
    // Badlands Generation
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(125, 150)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Center)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTrc', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), GetRandomReal(1.00, 1.35), GetRandomInt(0, 5))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(30, 40)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Center)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsh', udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING, GetRandomReal(0.80, 1.20), GetRandomInt(0, 7))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Center)
    call EnumDestructablesInCircleBJ(200.00, udg_TempPoint, function Trig_Initialization_Func151A)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ngol', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call SetResourceAmount(GetLastCreatedUnit(), 4800)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(4, 7)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Center)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkob', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(2, 4)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Center)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkot', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    //  
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(75, 125)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Bottom)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTrc', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), GetRandomReal(1.00, 1.35), GetRandomInt(0, 5))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(15, 30)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Bottom)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsh', udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING, GetRandomReal(0.80, 1.20), GetRandomInt(0, 7))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(2, 4)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Bottom)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkob', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 2)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Bottom)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkot', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    //  
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(50, 75)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Right)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTrc', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), GetRandomReal(1.00, 1.35), GetRandomInt(0, 5))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(10, 15)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Right)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsh', udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING, GetRandomReal(0.80, 1.20), GetRandomInt(0, 7))
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 2)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_TempInt
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Right)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkob', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Desert_Mine_Right)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00K', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'n00I', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkot', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    //  
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_North_Badlands_Spawn)
    call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint, 'Vgrs', - 1, 1, 0)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncnt', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(6, 10)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(udg_TempInt, 'ncea', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncen', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncks', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_TempLoc=OffsetLocation(udg_TempPoint, 150.00, 150.00)
    call CreateDestructableLoc('YT15', udg_TempLoc, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
    call CreateDestructableLoc('XOk2', udg_TempLoc, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    //  
    set udg_TempLoc=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_South_Badlands_Spawn)
    call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempLoc, 'Vgrs', - 1, 1, 0)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nct2', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(6, 10)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(udg_TempInt, 'ncea', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncim', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncnk', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_TempPoint=OffsetLocation(udg_TempLoc, - 150.00, - 150.00)
    call CreateDestructableLoc('YT15', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
    call CreateDestructableLoc('XOk2', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    // Forest Generation
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Fountain_3)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func209C() ) then
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nfoh', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func209Func001C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nmoo', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ndfl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Fountain_2)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func213C() ) then
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nfoh', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func213Func001C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nmoo', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ndfl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Fountain_1)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
    if ( Trig_Initialization_Func217C() ) then
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nfoh', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        if ( Trig_Initialization_Func217Func001C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nmoo', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ndfl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    // Objectives and Help
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2551", "TRIGSTR_2552", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNUpgradeRegenerationAura.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2553", "TRIGSTR_2554", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNAnimateDead.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2557", "TRIGSTR_2558", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNStatUp.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2555", "TRIGSTR_2556", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNChestOfGold.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_3857", "TRIGSTR_3858", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNPickUpItem.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2565", "TRIGSTR_2566", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNImprovedStrengthOfTheWild.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_3544", "TRIGSTR_3545", "war3mapImported\\BTNFood_FlowerDaisy.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2567", "TRIGSTR_2568", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNOrcMeleeUpOne.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2569", "TRIGSTR_2570", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNGatherGold.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2561", "TRIGSTR_2562", "war3mapImported\\BTNMisc_Shovel.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2563", "TRIGSTR_2564", "war3mapImported\\BTNMisc_Fishing.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2559", "TRIGSTR_2560", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNBlacksmith.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2575", "TRIGSTR_2576", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNStaffOfPreservation.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2577", "TRIGSTR_2578", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNHumanCaptureFlag.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2579", "TRIGSTR_2580", "ReplaceableTextures\\WorldEditUI\\Editor-MultipleDoodads.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_3519", "TRIGSTR_3520", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNAuraOfDarkness.blp")
    call CreateQuestBJ(bj_QUESTTYPE_REQ_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2581", "TRIGSTR_2582", "ReplaceableTextures\\WorldEditUI\\Editor-Random-Unit.blp")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Initialization takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Initialization=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Initialization, function Trig_Initialization_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Multiboard
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[8] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(7)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[7] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(6)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[6] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(5)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[5] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(4)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[4] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(3)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[3] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(2)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then

    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false

    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[2] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(1)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

function Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MultiboardPlayer[1] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(0)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func023Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nmrk' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nshp' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'haro' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func023Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Multiboard_Func023Func001Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Func023A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func023Func001C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())
        call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempPoint, 5.00)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Multiboard_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call PlayMusicBJ(gg_snd_Comradeship)
    // Multiboard Setup
    call CreateMultiboardBJ(5, ( udg_PlayerCount + 1 ), "TRIGSTR_2583")
    set udg_Multiboard=GetLastCreatedMultiboard()
    call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_Multiboard, 0, 0, true, false)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, 1, 10.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, 1, 6.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, 1, 6.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, 1, 6.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, 1, 4.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, 1, "TRIGSTR_2584")
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, 1, "TRIGSTR_2585")
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, 1, "TRIGSTR_2575")
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, 1, "TRIGSTR_2577")
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, 1, "TRIGSTR_2588")
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_PlayerCount
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=false
        if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002C() ) then
            set udg_MultiboardPlayer[1]=true
            set udg_PlayerRow[1]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
            set udg_TempInt=1
            set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
        else
            if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001C() ) then
                set udg_MultiboardPlayer[2]=true
                set udg_PlayerRow[2]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                set udg_TempInt=2
                set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
            else
                if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_MultiboardPlayer[3]=true
                    set udg_PlayerRow[3]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                    set udg_TempInt=3
                    set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                else
                    if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_MultiboardPlayer[4]=true
                        set udg_PlayerRow[4]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                        set udg_TempInt=4
                        set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            set udg_MultiboardPlayer[5]=true
                            set udg_PlayerRow[5]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                            set udg_TempInt=5
                            set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                set udg_MultiboardPlayer[6]=true
                                set udg_PlayerRow[6]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                                set udg_TempInt=6
                                set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    set udg_MultiboardPlayer[7]=true
                                    set udg_PlayerRow[7]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                                    set udg_TempInt=7
                                    set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Multiboard_Func016Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        set udg_MultiboardPlayer[8]=true
                                        set udg_PlayerRow[8]=( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 )
                                        set udg_TempInt=8
                                        set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=true
                                    else
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
        set udg_PlayerStatus[udg_TempInt]="|c0096FF96Alive|r"
        set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFF949694Trusted|r"
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(gg_unit_nbsm_0002, ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt))
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), 10.00)
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), 6.00)
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), 6.00)
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), 6.00)
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), 4.00)
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), ( ( udg_PlayerColor[udg_TempInt] + GetPlayerName(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt)) ) + "|r" ))
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), udg_PlayerStatus[udg_TempInt])
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), I2S(udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt]))
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt])
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), I2S(udg_Kills[udg_TempInt]))
        set udg_MultiboardPlaceCheck=false
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ(false, udg_Multiboard)
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ(true, udg_Multiboard)
    call TriggerSleepAction(15.00)
    call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_DISCOVERED, "TRIGSTR_2591")
    call FlashQuestDialogButtonBJ()
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectOfPlayer(gg_rct_Sanctuary, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Multiboard_Func023A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Multiboard takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Multiboard=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventSingle(gg_trg_Multiboard, 0.01)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Multiboard, function Trig_Multiboard_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Timer On
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Timer_On_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Item_Cleanup)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Timer_1_Sec)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Timer_5_Sec)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Zombie_AI)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Timer_On takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Timer_On=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterGameLoadedEventBJ(gg_trg_Timer_On)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Timer_On, function Trig_Timer_On_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Timer 1 Sec
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TimeSeconds == 10 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TimeSeconds_Tens == 6 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TimeMinutes == 10 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TimeMinutes_Tens == 6 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002Func003Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetEnumUnit()) != String2OrderIdBJ("move") ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetEnumUnit()) != String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002Func003Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'H00F' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(GetEnumUnit(), 'Bspe') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001C() ) then
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_TrampleGroup)
    else
        if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003C() ) then
            call SetUnitPathing(GetEnumUnit(), true)
            if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007Func001Func003Func002Func003C() ) then
                    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A03L', GetEnumUnit())
                    call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_TrampleGroup)
                else
                endif
            else
                call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A02A', GetEnumUnit())
                call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_TrampleGroup)
            endif
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Multiboard Clock
    set udg_TimeSeconds=( udg_TimeSeconds + 1 )
    if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_TimeSeconds=0
        set udg_TimeSeconds_Tens=( udg_TimeSeconds_Tens + 1 )
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func004C() ) then
        set udg_TimeSeconds_Tens=0
        set udg_TimeMinutes=( udg_TimeMinutes + 1 )
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func005C() ) then
        set udg_TimeMinutes=0
        set udg_TimeMinutes_Tens=( udg_TimeMinutes_Tens + 1 )
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func006C() ) then
        set udg_TimeMinutes_Tens=0
        set udg_TimeHours=( udg_TimeHours + 1 )
    else
    endif
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TrampleGroup, function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Func007A)
    set udg_Time=( I2S(udg_TimeHours) + ( ":" + ( I2S(udg_TimeMinutes_Tens) + ( I2S(udg_TimeMinutes) + ( ":" + ( I2S(udg_TimeSeconds_Tens) + I2S(udg_TimeSeconds) ) ) ) ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetTitleText(udg_Multiboard, ( "Zombies Remaining: |CFFFF0000" + ( ( I2S(udg_ZombieCount) + "|r" ) + ( " - Time: |c00FFFFFF" + ( udg_Time + "|r" ) ) ) ))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Timer_1_Sec takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Timer_1_Sec=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Timer_1_Sec)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Timer_1_Sec, 1.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Timer_1_Sec, function Trig_Timer_1_Sec_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func006Func001C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func006Func001Func001C() ) then
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(3, GetEnumPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
        else
            if ( Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func006Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(2, GetEnumPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
            else
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(1, GetEnumPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Anti-Spam Reset
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=8
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set udg_AntiSpam[GetForLoopIndexA()]=false
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    // Destructables
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_ZombieGroup, function Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func004A)
    // Income
    call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Func006A)
endfunction

    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Timer_5_Sec, 5.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Timer_5_Sec, function Trig_Timer_5_Sec_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Assault
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Assault_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitEnemy(GetAttacker(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetAttacker(), UNIT_TYPE_GROUND) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_ATTACKS_GROUND) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) != String2OrderIdBJ("attack") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetAttacker(), UNIT_TYPE_FLYING) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_ATTACKS_FLYING) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetTriggerUnit()) != String2OrderIdBJ("attack") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00P' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00N' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'e005' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o009' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'e004' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o00B' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00Q' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00O' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'u00B' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Func001Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assault_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Assault_Func001C() ) then
        call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(GetAttacker(), "stop")
    else
        if ( Trig_Assault_Func001Func005C() ) then
            call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(GetAttacker(), "stop")
        else
            if ( Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func001C() ) then
                call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "attack", GetAttacker())
            else
                if ( Trig_Assault_Func001Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "attack", GetAttacker())
                else
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Assault takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Assault=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Assault, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Assault, Condition(function Trig_Assault_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Assault, function Trig_Assault_Actions)
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

function Trig_Changing_Heroes_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002C() ) then
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 1), GetSoldUnit())
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 2), GetSoldUnit())
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 3), GetSoldUnit())
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 4), GetSoldUnit())
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 5), GetSoldUnit())
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetBuyingUnit(), 6), GetSoldUnit())
        set udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))]=GetSoldUnit()
        call RemoveUnit(GetBuyingUnit())
        if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func012C() ) then
            call SetHeroLevelBJ(GetSoldUnit(), GetHeroLevel(GetBuyingUnit()), false)
        else
            if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func012Func001C() ) then
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('cosl', GetSoldUnit())
            else
            endif
        endif
        call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], true, true)
        if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014C() ) then
            call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNTheCaptain.blp")
        else
            if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001C() ) then
                call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNPeasant.blp")
            else
                if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNShandris.blp")
                else
                    if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNFelGuardBlue.blp")
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNKnight.blp")
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNWitchDoctor.blp")
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNSpellBreaker.blp")
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNBloodElfPeasant.blp")
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                            call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNRifleman.blp")
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNAssassin.blp")
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Changing_Heroes_Func002Func014Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                    call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNAcolyte.blp")
                                                else
                                                    call MultiboardSetItemIconBJ(udg_Multiboard, 1, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))], "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNOrcWarlockRed.blp")
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetSoldUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetSoldUnit()))
    else
        call RemoveUnit(GetSoldUnit())
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(500, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
    endif
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

        return true
    endif
    if ( ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ZombiePlayers) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false

function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func011Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Defeat_Func002Func011Func001Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func011A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Defeat_Func002Func011Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitAnimation(GetEnumUnit(), "victory")
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func015A takes nothing returns nothing
    call CustomDefeatBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), "TRIGSTR_2976")
endfunction

function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func016A takes nothing returns nothing
    call CustomVictoryBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), true, true)
endfunction

function Trig_Defeat_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedAshwell == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedMoladune == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedRaiderOutpost == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedSanctuary == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Victory == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Defeat_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TownCount=( udg_TownCount - 1 )
    if ( Trig_Defeat_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_Victory=true
        call TriggerSleepAction(2)
        call PauseAllUnitsBJ(true)
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect())
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func011A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_ALWAYSHINT, "TRIGSTR_2978")
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func015A)
        call ForForce(udg_ZombiePlayers, function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func016A)
    else
        if ( Trig_Defeat_Func002Func002C() ) then
            call ForForce(udg_ZombiePlayers, function Trig_Defeat_Func002Func002Func001A)
        else
            if ( Trig_Defeat_Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_WARNING, "TRIGSTR_3003")
            else
                call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_ALWAYSHINT, ( "There are |c00FFFF00" + ( I2S(udg_TownCount) + "|r towns left." ) ))
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Defeat takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Defeat=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Defeat, function Trig_Defeat_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Victory
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Victory_Func001Func006001002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_Func001Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetEnumUnit(), "victory")
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_Func001Func009A takes nothing returns nothing
    call CustomVictoryBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), true, true)
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_Func001Func010A takes nothing returns nothing
    call CustomDefeatBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), "TRIGSTR_3528")
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_GraveyardGroup) <= 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(udg_Necromancer) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Victory == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Victory_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_Victory=true
        set udg_ZombieCount=0
        call TriggerSleepAction(2)
        call PauseAllUnitsBJ(true)
        set udg_ZombieCount=0
        call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Victory_Func001Func006001002)), function Trig_Victory_Func001Func006A)
        call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_ALWAYSHINT, "TRIGSTR_3527")
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Victory_Func001Func009A)
        call ForForce(udg_ZombiePlayers, function Trig_Victory_Func001Func010A)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Victory takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Victory=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Victory, function Trig_Victory_Actions)
endfunction
