function Trig_Kills_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Builder Lightsource
    if ( Trig_Kills_Func002C() ) then
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_LightCounter
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Kills_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveDestructable(LoadDestructableHandleBJ(GetForLoopIndexA(), 1, udg_FireHashtable))
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
    else
    endif
    // Destroyed Towns: Moladune
    if ( Trig_Kills_Func004C() ) then
        set udg_DestroyedMoladune=true
        call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'CObo', gg_rct_Moladune)
        call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSin', gg_rct_Moladune)
        call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LOar', gg_rct_Moladune)
        call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'LSba', gg_rct_Moladune)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_n00O_0009)
        call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsp', udg_TempPoint, GetUnitFacing(gg_unit_n00O_0009), 1.00, 0)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        call RemoveDestructable(gg_dest_DTlv_0046)
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_DESTROY, gg_dest_ITg4_0345)
        call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(gg_rct_Moladune, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func013A)
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Moladune)
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func015A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Blight_1)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Blight_2)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Blight_3)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u00B', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetLastCreatedUnit(), false)
        call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Blight_4)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_3004")
        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Defeat)
    else
        // Sanctuary
        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002C() ) then
            set udg_DestroyedSanctuary=true
            call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'CObo', gg_rct_Sanctuary)
            call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSin', gg_rct_Sanctuary)
            call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSgr', gg_rct_Sanctuary)
            call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSwm', gg_rct_Sanctuary)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_nshp_0069)
            call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsp', udg_TempPoint, GetUnitFacing(gg_unit_nshp_0069), 1.00, 0)
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            call RemoveDestructable(gg_dest_DTlv_2537)
            call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_DESTROY, gg_dest_LTg4_0633)
            call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(gg_dest_LTg4_0633, "death")
            call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(gg_rct_Sanctuary, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func014A)
            set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Sanctuary)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func016A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_1)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_2)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u00B', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetLastCreatedUnit(), false)
            call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_3)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_4)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_5)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_11)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_6)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_7)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_8)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Blight_9)
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Cathedral)
            call CreateDestructableLoc('ITag', udg_TempPoint, 270.00, 1.70, 0)
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_3005")
            call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Defeat)
        else
            // Raider's Outpost
            if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002C() ) then
                set udg_DestroyedRaiderOutpost=true
                call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'DRrk', gg_rct_Raiders_Outpost)
                call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LZth', gg_rct_Raiders_Outpost)
                call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSwm', gg_rct_Raiders_Outpost)
                call RemoveDestructable(gg_dest_DTlv_1763)
                call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_DESTROY, gg_dest_DTg4_1762)
                call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(gg_dest_DTg4_1762, "death")
                set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Raiders_Outpost)
                call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func011A)
                call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Raiders_Outpost_Blight_1)
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Orc)
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_6)
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u00B', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetLastCreatedUnit(), false)
                call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_3007")
                call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Defeat)
            else
                // Ashwell
                if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_DestroyedAshwell=true
                    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'CObo', gg_rct_Ashwell)
                    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSin', gg_rct_Ashwell)
                    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSgr', gg_rct_Ashwell)
                    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LSwm', gg_rct_Ashwell)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_n00P_0135)
                    call CreateDestructableLoc('DTsp', udg_TempPoint, GetUnitFacing(gg_unit_nshp_0069), 1.00, 0)
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    call RemoveDestructable(gg_dest_DTlv_4009)
                    call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_DESTROY, gg_dest_LTe2_4003)
                    call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(gg_dest_LTe2_4003, "death")
                    call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(gg_dest_LTex_3545, "death")
                    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Ashwell)
                    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func016A)
                    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Elf)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u00B', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetLastCreatedUnit(), false)
                    call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_1)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_2)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_3)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_4)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_5)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_6)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Blight_7)
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00V', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_3008")
                    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Defeat)
                else
                    // Boss Loot
                    if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
                        call CreateItemLoc('gold', udg_TempPoint)
                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func006C() ) then
                            call CreateItemLoc(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(5, ITEM_TYPE_PURCHASABLE), udg_TempPoint)
                        else
                            call CreateItemLoc(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(2, ITEM_TYPE_PURCHASABLE), udg_TempPoint)
                        endif
                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func007C() ) then
                            call CreateItemLoc('gold', udg_TempPoint)
                            call CreateItemLoc('gold', udg_TempPoint)
                        else
                        endif
                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    else
                        // Bone Dragon Spawn
                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                            set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
                            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'u003', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetUnitFacing(GetTriggerUnit()))
                            call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("chest", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Undead\\Darksummoning\\DarkSummonTarget.mdl")
                            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
                            call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetLastCreatedUnit(), udg_ZombieGroup)
                            set udg_ZombieCount=CountUnitsInGroup(udg_ZombieGroup)
                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                        else
                            // Zombie Kill Count
                            if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011C() ) then
                                if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func003C() ) then
                                    set udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] + 1 )
                                    set udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] + 50 )
                                    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))], I2S(udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]))
                                    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))], I2S(udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]))
                                    // Reputation Threshold Check
                                    set udg_TempPlayer=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ())
                                    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Reputation_Check)
                                else
                                endif
                                if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func004C() ) then
                                    set udg_ZombieCount=( udg_ZombieCount - 1 )
                                    call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_ZombieGroup)
                                    if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func004Func005C() ) then
                                        set udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] + 1 )
                                        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 5, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))], I2S(udg_Kills[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]))
                                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func004Func005Func003C() ) then
                                            set udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] + ( GetUnitLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 3 ) )
                                            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))], I2S(udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]))
                                        else
                                        endif
                                        // Reputation Threshold Check
                                        set udg_TempPlayer=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ())
                                        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Reputation_Check)
                                    else
                                    endif
                                else
                                endif
                                // Victory Check
                                if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func006C() ) then
                                    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Victory)
                                else
                                endif
                            else
                                // Player Death
                                if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002C() ) then
                                    set udg_PlayerStatus[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]="|c00FF7F00Dead|r"
                                    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], udg_PlayerStatus[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))])
                                    call TriggerSleepAction(6.00)
                                    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
                                    if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func006C() ) then
                                        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, 0)
                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3936")
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func006Func001C() ) then
                                            call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, ( 75 + ( 25 * GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) ) ))
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3937")
                                        else
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
                                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Hero_Revive)
                                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nbse', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                                    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
                                    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, 0.50)
                                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func001C() ) then
                                        call TriggerSleepAction(6.00)
                                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nbse', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_DeathPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                                        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
                                        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_DeathPoint, 0.50)
                                    else
                                        // Murder
                                        if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
                                            if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
                                                set udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] - 100 )
                                            else
                                                set udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]=( udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))] - 50 )
                                            endif
                                            if ( Trig_Kills_Func004Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func011Func002Func001Func002Func003C() ) then
                                                set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
                                                call CreateItemLoc('kysn', udg_TempPoint)
                                                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                            else
                                            endif
                                            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))], I2S(udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()))]))
                                            // Reputation Threshold Check
                                            set udg_TempPlayer=GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ())
                                            call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Reputation_Check)
                                        else
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Kills takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Kills=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Kills, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Kills, function Trig_Kills_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Leavers
//
// For them dirty deserters.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Leavers_Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetTriggerPlayer(), udg_ZombiePlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Leavers_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'ncop' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Leavers_Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Leavers_Func002Func001C() ) then
        call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
    else
        if ( Trig_Leavers_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
            call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), Player(11), true)
        else
            call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), Player(8), true)
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Leavers_Func005Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call CustomVictoryBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), true, true)
endfunction

function Trig_Leavers_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers) <= 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Leavers_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(GetTriggerPlayer())
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Leavers_Func002A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call ForceRemovePlayerSimple(GetTriggerPlayer(), udg_NeutralPlayers)
    if ( Trig_Leavers_Func005C() ) then
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        call ForForce(udg_ZombiePlayers, function Trig_Leavers_Func005Func002A)
    else
    endif
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], "TRIGSTR_2863")
    call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_UNITACQUIRED, ( ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r" ) ) + " has left the game." ))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Leavers takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Leavers=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(0))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(1))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(2))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(3))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(4))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(5))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(6))
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Leavers, Player(7))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Leavers, function Trig_Leavers_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Light of the Day
//
// Lowlands:
// 0 = fog, 1 = rain, 2 = light
// Highlands:
// 3 = wind, 4 = rain, 5 = light
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func012C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedSanctuary == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func018C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedMoladune == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func019C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedAshwell == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func020C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedRaiderOutpost == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func034002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit())) == MAP_CONTROL_USER )
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func035C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetFilterUnit(), 'sbok') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func037Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetEnumItem()) == 'sbok' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func037A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func037Func001C() ) then
        call SetItemCharges(GetEnumItem(), 3)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITx4' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LTt1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT13' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'DTes' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LTt0' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsDestructableDeadBJ(GetEnumDestructable()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT15' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT06' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001C() ) then
        call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), "death")
    else
        if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038Func001Func001C() ) then
            call DestructableRestoreLife(GetEnumDestructable(), GetDestructableMaxLife(GetEnumDestructable()), true)
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func041C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_EventVerdantRain == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    if ( not ( udg_EventVerdantRain == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

    if ( not ( udg_Weather_Current == 1 ) ) then
        return false

    if ( not ( udg_EventVerdantRain == true ) ) then

    if ( not ( udg_TempInt != udg_Weather_Current ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Weather == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Transition
    call CinematicFadeBJ(bj_CINEFADETYPE_FADEIN, 2.00, "ReplaceableTextures\\CameraMasks\\White_mask.blp", 100.00, 100.00, 100.00, 0.00)
    call SetDayNightModels("Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronTerrain\\DNCLordaeronTerrain.mdx", "Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronUnit\\DNCLordaeronUnit.mdx")
    call EnableUserUI(true)
    call ResetTerrainFogBJ()
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LOtz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LOlp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'LObz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'NOfp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("death", 'CPct', GetPlayableMapRect())
    // Respawns
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func012C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_1)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlk', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_2)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvk2', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_7)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvk2', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_11)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlk', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_12)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvk2', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_3)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlk', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func018C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_4)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(3, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func019C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_5)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(4, 'nhem', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func020C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_6)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(4, 'o00D', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_8)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvk2', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_9)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvlw', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Villager_Spawn_10)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'nhef', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nvil', Player(8), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func034002002))
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func035C() ) then
        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetFilterUnit(), 'sbok'), 3)
    else
    endif
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call EnumItemsInRectBJ(GetPlayableMapRect(), function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func037A)
    call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect(), function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func038A)
    // Weather
    call StopMusicBJ(false)
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func041C() ) then
        call PlayMusicBJ(gg_snd_VerdantRain)
        set udg_TempInt=1
    else
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(0, 3)
        call PlayMusicBJ("music")
    endif
    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func002C() ) then
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[udg_Weather_Current], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 3 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 6 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 9 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 12 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 15 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 18 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 21 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 24 )], false)
            else
                if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 8000.00, 1.00, 0.00, 100.00, 0.00)
                    else
                        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 8000.00, 1.00, 0.00, 0.00, 100.00)
                    endif
                else
                endif
            endif
            if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func003C() ) then
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[udg_TempInt], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 3 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 6 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 9 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 12 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 15 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 18 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 21 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 24 )], true)
                if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func003Func011C() ) then
                    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_RollingThunder1)
                    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func003Func011Func003C() ) then
                        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 8000.00, 1.00, 0.00, 100.00, 0.00)
                    else
                        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 8000.00, 1.00, 0.00, 0.00, 100.00)
                    endif
                else
                    if ( Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Func042Func001Func003Func011Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_North_Badlands_Spawn)
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ntor', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                        call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(600.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_West_Badlands_Spawn)
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ntor', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                        call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(600.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            else
            endif
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
    set udg_Weather_Current=udg_TempInt
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Light_of_the_Day takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Light_of_the_Day=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterGameStateEventTimeOfDay(gg_trg_Light_of_the_Day, EQUAL, 6.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Light_of_the_Day, function Trig_Light_of_the_Day_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Dark of the Night
//
// Lowlands:
// 0 = fog, 1 = rain, 2 = light
// Highlands:
// 3 = wind, 4 = rain, 5 = light
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT15' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT06' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010Func001C() ) then
        call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), "stand")
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nhef' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nvlw' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nhem' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nvlk' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nvk2' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nvil' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'o00D' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012Func001C() ) then
        call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func016C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_EventBloodMoon == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func011C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Weather_Current < 3 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012Func011Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012Func011C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt < 3 ) ) then
        return false
    endif

endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt != udg_Weather_Current ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Weather == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Transition
    call CinematicFadeBJ(bj_CINEFADETYPE_FADEIN, 2.00, "ReplaceableTextures\\CameraMasks\\Black_mask.blp", 100.00, 100.00, 100.00, 0.00)
    call SetDayNightModels("", "")
    call EnableUserUI(true)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'LOtz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'LObz', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'LOlp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'NOfp', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("stand", 'CPct', GetPlayableMapRect())
    call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect(), function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func010A)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(Player(8))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func012A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    // Blood Moon
    call StopMusicBJ(false)
    if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func016C() ) then
        call PlayMusicBJ(gg_snd_BloodMoon)
        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 6000.00, 1.00, 40.00, 0.00, 0.00)
    else
        call SetTerrainFogExBJ(0, 0.00, 6000.00, 1.00, 0.00, 0.00, 20.00)
        call PlayMusicBJ(gg_snd_SadMystery)
    endif
    // Weather
    if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018C() ) then
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(0, 3)
        if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func011C() ) then
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[udg_Weather_Current], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 3 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 6 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 9 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 12 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 15 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 18 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 21 )], false)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_Weather_Current + 24 )], false)
            else
            endif
            if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012C() ) then
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[udg_TempInt], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 3 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 6 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 9 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 12 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 15 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 18 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 21 )], true)
                call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[( udg_TempInt + 24 )], true)
                if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012Func011C() ) then
                    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_RollingThunder1)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Func018Func002Func012Func011Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_North_Badlands_Spawn)
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ntor', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                        call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(600.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                        set udg_TempPoint=GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_West_Badlands_Spawn)
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ntor', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                        call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(600.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            else
            endif
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[2], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[5], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[8], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[11], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[14], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[17], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[20], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[23], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[26], false)
            set udg_Weather_Current=udg_TempInt
        else
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[2], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[5], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[8], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[11], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[14], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[17], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[20], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[23], false)
            call EnableWeatherEffect(udg_Weather_Effects[26], false)
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Dark_of_the_Night takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Dark_of_the_Night=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterGameStateEventTimeOfDay(gg_trg_Dark_of_the_Night, EQUAL, 18.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Dark_of_the_Night, function Trig_Dark_of_the_Night_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Respawn Animals
//
// Revives anything as is in the original starting spot.
// May or may not work with exploded units...
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'necr' ) ) then
        return true

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nrac' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nder' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshe' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'npig' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nech' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nhmc' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'ncrb' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nskk' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nfro' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nrat' ) ) then
        return true

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00K' ) ) then
        return true

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00I' ) ) then
        return true

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n006' ) ) then
        return true

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nwlg' ) ) then

endfunction

    if ( not Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func001C() ) then

    if ( not Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'necr' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nrac' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nder' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nwlg' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call TriggerSleepAction(120.00)
    if ( Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
        if ( Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func003C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nder', Player(bj_PLAYER_NEUTRAL_VICTIM), udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        else
            if ( Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func003Func001C() ) then
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nwlg', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            else
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'necr', Player(bj_PLAYER_NEUTRAL_VICTIM), udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            endif
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Respawn_Animals_Func003Func001C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()), Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()), Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        endif
    endif
    call SetUnitUserData(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_CreepPoint[GetUnitUserData(GetTriggerUnit())], "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\Heal\\HealTarget.mdl")
    set udg_SpecialFX=GetLastCreatedEffectBJ()
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Special_Effect_Destruction)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Respawn_Animals takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Respawn_Animals=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Respawn_Animals, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Respawn_Animals, Condition(function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Respawn_Animals, function Trig_Respawn_Animals_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Revive
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Revive_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != Player(11) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Revive_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Revive_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetRevivingUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), 'nbse')
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Revive_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    set udg_PlayerStatus[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]="|c0096FF96Alive|r"
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], udg_PlayerStatus[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))])
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, 0.50)
    set udg_TempInt=GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Revive takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Revive=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Revive, EVENT_PLAYER_HERO_REVIVE_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Revive, Condition(function Trig_Revive_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Revive, function Trig_Revive_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Rotate Structure
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A005' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_PlayerRotate[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetRandomInt(1, 2) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00W' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetRandomInt(1, 2) == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h008' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_PlayerRotate[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
    set udg_TempReal=GetUnitFacing(GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    if ( Trig_Rotate_Structure_Func004C() ) then
        call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'n00W', bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
        call SetUnitPositionLocFacingBJ(GetLastReplacedUnitBJ(), udg_TempPoint, ( udg_TempReal + 45.00 ))
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastReplacedUnitBJ(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
        if ( Trig_Rotate_Structure_Func004Func001C() ) then
            call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'h008', bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
            call SetUnitPositionLocFacingBJ(GetLastReplacedUnitBJ(), udg_TempPoint, ( udg_TempReal + 45.00 ))
            call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastReplacedUnitBJ(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        else
            call SetUnitPositionLocFacingBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_TempPoint, ( udg_TempReal + 45.00 ))
        endif
    endif
    set udg_PlayerRotate[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=false
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Rotate_Structure takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Rotate_Structure=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Rotate_Structure, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Rotate_Structure, Condition(function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Rotate_Structure, function Trig_Rotate_Structure_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetSoldItem()) == 'guvi' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("chest", GetBuyingUnit(), "UI\\Feedback\\GoldCredit\\GoldCredit.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func002C() ) then
            set udg_UpgradeWeapons=( udg_UpgradeWeapons + 1 )
            call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func002Func007A)
            call ForForce(udg_Townsfolk, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func002Func008A)
            call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_UNITACQUIRED, ( "The |c007d7d7dTownsfolk's|r weapons have improved to tier " + ( I2S(udg_UpgradeWeapons) + "." ) ))
        else
            set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3027")
            call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(350, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(250, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func002C() ) then
                set udg_UpgradeArmor=( udg_UpgradeArmor + 1 )
                call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func002Func007A)
                call ForForce(udg_Townsfolk, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func002Func008A)
                call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_UNITACQUIRED, ( "The |c007d7d7dTownsfolk's|r armor has improved to tier " + ( I2S(udg_UpgradeArmor) + "." ) ))
            else
                set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3028")
                call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(300, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(300, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_UpgradeStructure=( udg_UpgradeStructure + 1 )
                    call ForForce(udg_NeutralPlayers, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func001Func001Func007A)
                    call ForForce(udg_Townsfolk, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Func003Func001Func001Func001Func008A)
                    call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_UNITACQUIRED, ( "The |c007d7d7dTownsfolk's|r structures have improved to tier " + ( I2S(udg_UpgradeStructure) + "." ) ))
                else
                    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3029")
                    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
                    call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(150, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
                    call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(350, GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Townsfolk_Upgrades takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Townsfolk_Upgrades=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Townsfolk_Upgrades, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SELL_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Townsfolk_Upgrades, function Trig_Townsfolk_Upgrades_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Zombify
//
// Defeat for last hunter here.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Zombify_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetResearched() == 'Rnsb' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] > - 500 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) == Player(11) ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()), udg_ZombiePlayers) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitAnimation(GetEnumUnit(), "victory")
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func019Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetPlayerHandicapXPBJ(GetEnumPlayer(), 50.00)
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func019C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_ZombieGroup) > CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_SUMMONED) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'ncop' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'nbse' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001C() ) then
        call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
    else
        if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func001C() ) then
            call DoNothing()
        else
            if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call KillUnit(GetEnumUnit())
            else
                call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), Player(8), true)
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func023Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'E003' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'H00F' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'H003' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'E002' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'H007' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) == 'H002' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func023C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Zombify_Func008Func023Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountPlayersInForceBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers) <= 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombify_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    set udg_PlayerStatus[udg_TempInt]="|c00FF0000Zombie|r"
    if ( Trig_Zombify_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt]=- 500
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, udg_PlayerRow[udg_TempInt], I2S(udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt]))
    else
    endif
    set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFFFF0000Hated|r"
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 2, udg_PlayerRow[udg_TempInt], udg_PlayerStatus[udg_TempInt])
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, udg_PlayerRow[udg_TempInt], udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt])
    call ForceRemovePlayerSimple(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers)
    if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_Victory=true
        call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_ALWAYSHINT, "TRIGSTR_3011")
        call PauseAllUnitsBJ(true)
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectAll(GetPlayableMapRect())
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func005A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        call CustomDefeatBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), "TRIGSTR_2976")
        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Defeat)
    else
        call ForceAddPlayerSimple(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_ZombiePlayers)
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, 0)
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), Player(11), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(11), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
        call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_ZombiePlayers, udg_NeutralPlayers, bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
        call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_NeutralPlayers, udg_ZombiePlayers, bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
        call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_ZombiePlayers, udg_Townsfolk, bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
        call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(udg_Townsfolk, udg_ZombiePlayers, bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
        call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_ALWAYSHINT, ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] + ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) + "|r has become a |c00FF0000Zombie|r." ) ))
        if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func019C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3933")
            call ForForce(udg_ZombiePlayers, function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func019Func002A)
            call SetPlayerHandicapXPBJ(Player(11), 50.00)
        else
        endif
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Zombify_Func008Func021A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        if ( Trig_Zombify_Func008Func023C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'U004', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_DeathPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'U006', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_DeathPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        endif
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt], GetRandomInt(1, 6)), GetLastCreatedUnit())
        call SetHeroLevelBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), ( GetHeroLevel(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]) / 2 ), false)
        call RemoveUnit(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt])
        set udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt]=GetLastCreatedUnit()
        call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(udg_PlayerHero[udg_TempInt], GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Undead\\RaiseSkeletonWarrior\\RaiseSkeleton.mdl")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_DeathPoint, 0.50)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Zombify takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Zombify=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Zombify, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_RESEARCH_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Zombify, Condition(function Trig_Zombify_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Zombify, function Trig_Zombify_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Conversations
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Conversations_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == Player(8) ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == Player(9) ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Conversations_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00S' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Conversations_Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkHostile[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetSpellTargetUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSpellTargetUnit()) != 'ndog' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Conversations_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(GetSpellTargetUnit(), "stop")
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
    // Child
    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010C() ) then
        call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatChild, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3253", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
    else
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 5)
        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002C() ) then
            // Positive Reply
            // Tinker
            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006C() ) then
                call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatTinker, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func005C() ) then
                    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3067", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func005Func001C() ) then
                        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3066", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func005Func001Func002C() ) then
                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3065", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func005Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3064", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                            else
                                call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3063", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            else
                // Dwarves
                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002C() ) then
                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func002C() ) then
                        call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatRifleman, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                            call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatMortarTeam, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                        else
                            call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatMountainKing, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                        endif
                    endif
                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func005C() ) then
                        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3062", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func005Func001C() ) then
                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3061", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func005Func001Func002C() ) then
                                call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3060", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func005Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3059", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                else
                                    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3058", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                else
                    // Elf Male
                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004C() ) then
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func002C() ) then
                            call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatElder, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func002Func001C() ) then

                            else

                            endif
                        endif
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func005C() ) then
                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3057", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func005Func001C() ) then
                                call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3056", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func005Func001Func002C() ) then
                                    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3055", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func005Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
