                                    else
                                        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3053", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    else
                        // Archer/Sorceress
                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004C() ) then
                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func001C() ) then

                            else
                                call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatSorceress, 75.00, udg_TempPoint, 0)

                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func005C() ) then

                        else

                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004C() ) then

                                    else

                                    endif
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004Func004Func002C() ) then

                                        else
                                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3125", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                        endif
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004Func004Func002Func001C() ) then
                                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3148", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004Func004Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004Func004Func002Func001Func002Func001C() ) then

                                                     call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)

                                                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func006Func002Func004Func004Func004Func004Func002Func001Func002Func002C() ) then

                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func003Func002Func004Func004Func005Func004Func003Func005Func003Func001C() ) then
                                                    call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3071", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                                else
                                                    if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func003Func002Func004Func004Func005Func004Func003Func005Func003Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                        call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3070", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                                    else
                                                        if ( Trig_Conversations_Func010Func002Func003Func002Func004Func004Func005Func004Func003Func005Func003Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                            call CreateTextTagLocBJ("TRIGSTR_3069", udg_TempPoint, 0, 10.00, 100, 100.00, 100.00, 0)
                                                        else

                        endif
                    endif

        endif
    endif
    set udg_TempFloatText=GetLastCreatedTextTag()

    call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(udg_TempFloatText, false)
    call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(udg_TempFloatText, 4.00)
    call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(udg_TempFloatText, 3.00)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)

        set udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=( udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] + 5 )
    else
    endif
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 3, udg_PlayerRow[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))], I2S(udg_Reputation[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]))
    // Reputation Threshold Check
    set udg_TempPlayer=GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Reputation_Check)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Conversations takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Conversations=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Conversations, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Conversations, Condition(function Trig_Conversations_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Conversations, function Trig_Conversations_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Reputation Check
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] >= 600 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] >= 300 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] < 600 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] >= 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] < 300 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] > - 250 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] < 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] > - 500 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] <= - 250 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] <= - 500 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkAllied[udg_TempInt] == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkHostile[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkAllied[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkHostile[udg_TempInt] == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001Func001C() ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001Func002C() ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkAllied[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkHostile[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] <= - 500 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] < 300 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] > - 500 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkAllied[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_TownsfolkHostile[udg_TempInt] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Reputation[udg_TempInt] >= 600 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Reputation_Check_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=GetConvertedPlayerId(udg_TempPlayer)
    if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFFFF0000Hated|r"
    else
        if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFFFF8A08Despised|r"
        else
            if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFFFFFF00Shady|r"
            else
                if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFF949694Trusted|r"
                else
                    if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFFA6FF4DAdmired|r"
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            set udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt]="|CFF18BE00Exalted|r"
                        else
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Multiboard, 4, udg_PlayerRow[udg_TempInt], udg_PlayerAlignment[udg_TempInt])
    if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004C() ) then
        set udg_TownsfolkAllied[udg_TempInt]=true
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(8), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(8), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(9), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
        call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(9), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
    else
        if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003C() ) then
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(8), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(8), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(9), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(9), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED)
        else
            if ( Trig_Reputation_Check_Func004Func003Func008C() ) then
                set udg_TownsfolkHostile[udg_TempInt]=true
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(8), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(8), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(Player(9), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
                call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), Player(9), bj_ALLIANCE_UNALLIED)
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Reputation_Check takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Reputation_Check=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Reputation_Check, function Trig_Reputation_Check_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Angry Forest
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Angry_Forest_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Forest_1, GetTriggerUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Forest_2, GetTriggerUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Angry_Forest_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("harvest") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Angry_Forest_Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetOrderTargetDestructable()) == 'ATtr' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetRandomInt(1, 4) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsPointBlightedBJ(udg_TempPoint) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Angry_Forest_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetDestructableLoc(GetOrderTargetDestructable())
    if ( Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006C() ) then
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
        if ( Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006Func002C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenp', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        else
            if ( Trig_Angry_Forest_Func006Func002Func001C() ) then
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nepl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            else
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenc', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            endif
        endif
    else
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'e006', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    endif
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "birth")
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\NightElf\\EntBirthTarget\\EntBirthTarget.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Angry_Forest takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Angry_Forest=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Angry_Forest, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Angry_Forest, Condition(function Trig_Angry_Forest_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Angry_Forest, function Trig_Angry_Forest_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Construction
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Construction_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) == GetOwningPlayer(GetConstructedStructure()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Construction_Func004Func001C() ) then
        call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 8 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetEnumUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetEnumUnit(), true)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetConstructedStructure()) == 'n002' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetConstructedStructure()) == 'n004' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetConstructedStructure()) == 'n00S' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func008Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetConstructedStructure()) == 'n005' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetConstructedStructure()) == 'n015' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Construction_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Builder Exp
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetConstructedStructure())
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(400.00, udg_TempPoint)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Construction_Func004A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    // Firepit Light
    if ( Trig_Construction_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_LightCounter=( udg_LightCounter + 1 )
        call SaveUnitHandleBJ(GetConstructedStructure(), udg_LightCounter, 0, udg_FireHashtable)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetConstructedStructure())
        call CreateDestructableLoc('XOk2', udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING, 1, 0)
        call SaveDestructableHandleBJ(GetLastCreatedDestructable(), udg_LightCounter, 1, udg_FireHashtable)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    else
        // Well Regen
        if ( Trig_Construction_Func008Func008C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A01L', GetConstructedStructure())
        else
            // Explosives
            if ( Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002C() ) then
                call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Amnz', GetConstructedStructure())
            else
                if ( Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002Func001C() ) then
                    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Amnx', GetConstructedStructure())
                else
                    // Lamp Fire Removal
                    if ( Trig_Construction_Func008Func008Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
                        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A014', GetConstructedStructure())
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Construction takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Construction=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Construction, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_CONSTRUCT_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Construction, function Trig_Construction_Actions)
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Digging_Func014Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) != 'Vcrp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) != 'Vcbp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) != 'Vstp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) != 'Vrck' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPointBlightedBJ(udg_TempPoint) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) != 'Glav' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Digging_Func014C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint) == 'Vdrt' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Digging_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Setup
    set udg_TempPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_TempPoint, "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\Undead\\ImpaleTargetDust\\ImpaleTargetDust.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 20)
    // Graveyard
    if ( Trig_Digging_Func008C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func003C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nskg', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        else
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n011', Player(11), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
        endif
        call SetUnitAnimation(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "birth")
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3387")
        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
    else
        // Common Items
        if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002C() ) then
            call CreateItemLoc('kysn', udg_TempPoint)
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3269")
            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
        else
            if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002C() ) then
                call CreateItemLoc('tgxp', udg_TempPoint)
                call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), 1)
                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3389")
                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
            else
                if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007C() ) then
                    if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func004C() ) then
                        call CreateItemLoc('sor8', udg_TempPoint)
                    else
                        call CreateItemLoc('sorf', udg_TempPoint)
                    endif
                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3390")
                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                else
                    // Random Monsters
                    if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003C() ) then
                        if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003Func003C() ) then
                            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nkob', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003Func003Func001C() ) then
                                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ngrk', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                            else
                                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nske', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                            endif
                            call SetUnitAnimation(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "birth")
                        endif
                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3391")
                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                    else
                        // Rare Items
                        if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003Func002C() ) then
                            if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003Func002Func002C() ) then
                                call CreateItemLoc(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(- 1, ITEM_TYPE_PERMANENT), udg_TempPoint)
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Digging_Func008Func002Func002Func007Func003Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                                    call CreateItemLoc('engs', udg_TempPoint)
                                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                else
                                    call CreateItemLoc(ChooseRandomItemExBJ(- 1, ITEM_TYPE_PURCHASABLE), udg_TempPoint)
                                endif
                            endif
                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3392")
                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                        else
                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3263")
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    // Hero Experience Gain
    if ( Trig_Digging_Func011C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Digging_Func011Func001C() ) then
            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 10 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 3 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
        else
            if ( Trig_Digging_Func011Func001Func002C() ) then
                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 15 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 4 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
            else
                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 2 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
    // Reset
    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=false
    if ( Trig_Digging_Func014C() ) then
        call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint, 'Vdrr', - 1, 1, 0)
    else
        if ( Trig_Digging_Func014Func001C() ) then
            call SetTerrainTypeBJ(udg_TempPoint, 'Vdrt', - 1, 1, 0)
        else
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Digging takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Digging=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Digging, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Digging, Condition(function Trig_Digging_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Digging, function Trig_Digging_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Fishing_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Setup
    call DestroyEffect(AddSpecialEffect("Abilities\\Spells\\Other\\CrushingWave\\CrushingWaveDamage.mdl", GetUnitX(GetSpellTargetUnit()), GetUnitY(GetSpellTargetUnit())))
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_TempPoint, "Abilities\\Spells\\Other\\CrushingWave\\CrushingWaveDamage.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 20)
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    // Fresh Water Spot
    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3358")
            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('shcw', GetTriggerUnit())
            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
        else
            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3359")
                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('anfg', GetTriggerUnit())
                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('anfg', GetTriggerUnit())
                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
            else
                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3360")
                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('anfg', GetTriggerUnit())
                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                else
                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003C() ) then
                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3361")
                        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('anfg', GetTriggerUnit())
                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003C() ) then
                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3362")
                            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wneg', GetTriggerUnit())
                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003C() ) then
                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3364")
                                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wneg', GetTriggerUnit())
                                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wneg', GetTriggerUnit())
                                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003C() ) then
                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3363")
                                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wneg', GetTriggerUnit())
                                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002C() ) then
                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3365")
                                        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002Func003C() ) then
                                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002Func003Func001C() ) then
                                                set udg_FishingBoot[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3366")
                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('btst', GetTriggerUnit())
                                            else
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3367")
                                                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                            endif
                                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002Func003Func003C() ) then
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3369")
                                                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002Func003Func003Func002C() ) then
                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3368")
                                                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rat3', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                else
                                                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func003Func006Func007Func003Func003Func003Func003Func002Func003Func003Func002Func002C() ) then
                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3370")
                                                        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
                                                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nmrl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                                                        call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatMurloc, 100, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                                                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                    else
                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3371")
                                                    endif
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    else
        // Ocean Spot
        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3372")
                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('tmmt', GetTriggerUnit())
                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
            else
                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3373")
                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('crys', GetTriggerUnit())
                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('crys', GetTriggerUnit())
                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                else
                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007C() ) then
                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3374")
                        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('crys', GetTriggerUnit())
                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005C() ) then
                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3375")
                            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('crys', GetTriggerUnit())
                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func005C() ) then
                                set udg_HydraFight=true
                                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Hydra_Spawn)
                                call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 3.00)
                                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nahy', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                                set udg_Hydra=GetLastCreatedUnit()
                                call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_Hydra, true)
                                call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatHydra, 100, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3376")
                                call TriggerSleepAction(3.00)
                                call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_Hydra, false)
                                call SetUnitOwner(udg_Hydra, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), true)
                            else
                            endif
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006C() ) then
                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3377")
                                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('thdm', GetTriggerUnit())
                                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005C() ) then
                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3378")
                                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('thdm', GetTriggerUnit())
                                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('thdm', GetTriggerUnit())
                                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007C() ) then
                                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func001C() ) then
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3379")
                                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('btst', GetTriggerUnit())
                                        else
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3380")
                                            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('thdm', GetTriggerUnit())
                                        endif
                                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func003C() ) then
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3381")
                                            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func003Func003C() ) then
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3382")
                                                call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func003Func003Func002C() ) then
                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3383")
                                                    call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wcyc', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                else
                                                    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func003Func003Func002Func002C() ) then
                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3384")
                                                        call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rat6', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                        set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                    else
                                                        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func003Func007Func007Func005Func006Func005Func007Func003Func003Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3385")
                                                            call SetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'), ( GetItemCharges(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp')) - 1 ))
                                                            set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
                                                            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nmrl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                                                            call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_WhatMurloc, 100, udg_TempPoint, 0)
                                                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                            set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
                                                        else
                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3386")
                                                        endif
                                                    endif
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        else
            // Fountain
            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func010Func002Func002C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3356")
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('kysn', GetTriggerUnit())
                set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
            else
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3357")
            endif
        endif
    endif
     call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    // Item Indexing
    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func013C() ) then
        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
    else
    endif
    // Hero Experience Gain
    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func015C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Fishing_Func015Func002C() ) then
            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 15 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 3 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
        else
            if ( Trig_Fishing_Func015Func002Func001C() ) then
                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 3 + GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
            else
                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 3 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
    // Reset
    set udg_GainExp[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=false
    if ( Trig_Fishing_Func018C() ) then
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tgxp'))
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Fishing takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Fishing=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Fishing, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Fishing, Condition(function Trig_Fishing_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Fishing, function Trig_Fishing_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Gathering
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Gathering_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("harvest") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gathering_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    // Builder Exp
    call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 2 + ( 1 / GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Gathering takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Gathering=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Gathering, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Gathering, Condition(function Trig_Gathering_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Gathering, function Trig_Gathering_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Hunting
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Hunting_Func001Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n006' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) != GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Hunting_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'necr' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nrac' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nder' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshe' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'npig' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( Trig_Hunting_Func001Func006C() ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nwlt' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nwlg' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nwld' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Hunting_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetKillingUnitBJ(), 'kgal') == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetKillingUnitBJ(), 'srtl') == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetKillingUnitBJ(), 'desc') == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif

function Trig_Hunting_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetKillingUnitBJ(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Hunting_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    if ( Trig_Hunting_Func004C() ) then
        call CreateItemLoc('sora', udg_TempPoint)
        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
        call CreateItemLoc('sor6', udg_TempPoint)
    else
        if ( Trig_Hunting_Func004Func001C() ) then
            call CreateItemLoc('sor5', udg_TempPoint)
        else
            if ( Trig_Hunting_Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
                call CreateItemLoc('sora', udg_TempPoint)
                call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), GetRandomInt(2, 3))
                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                call CreateItemLoc('sor7', udg_TempPoint)
            else
                if ( Trig_Hunting_Func004Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
                    call CreateItemLoc('sor6', udg_TempPoint)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Hunting_Func004Func001Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                        call CreateItemLoc('sora', udg_TempPoint)
                        call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), 2)
                    else
                        call CreateItemLoc('sora', udg_TempPoint)
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    // Hero Experience Gain
    if ( Trig_Hunting_Func008C() ) then
        call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 15 - GetHeroLevel(GetKillingUnitBJ()) ), GetKillingUnitBJ(), true)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Hunting takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Hunting=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Hunting, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Hunting, Condition(function Trig_Hunting_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Hunting, function Trig_Hunting_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004Func001C() ) then
        call KillDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('iwbr', GetTriggerUnit())
        call AddHeroXPSwapped(( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 3 ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3505")
        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004Func001Func005C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004Func001Func005Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004Func001Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenp', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                else
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenc', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                endif
            else
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'e006', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            endif
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction
