function Trig_Interact_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002C() ) then
        // Consumables
        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004C() ) then
            call KillDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
            call RemoveDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('cosl', GetTriggerUnit())
            call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3461")
        else
            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rej2', GetTriggerUnit())
                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3460")
            else
                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004C() ) then
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetDestructableLoc(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                    call RemoveDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                    call CreateDestructableLoc('ITx3', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1.10, 0)
                    call SetDestructableInvulnerableBJ(GetLastCreatedDestructable(), true)
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('shrs', GetTriggerUnit())
                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3459")
                else
                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001C() ) then
                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ram3', GetTriggerUnit())
                        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3420")
                    else
                        // Gathering
                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
                            call KillDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func004C() ) then
                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('wtlg', GetTriggerUnit())
                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3468")
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func004Func001C() ) then
                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('thle', GetTriggerUnit())
                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3467")
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func004Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('dphe', GetTriggerUnit())
                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3466")
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func004Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('bzbf', GetTriggerUnit())
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3465")
                                        else
                                            call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('shwd', GetTriggerUnit())
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3464")
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                            call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 3 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetSpellTargetUnit(), 0)
                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ram2', GetTriggerUnit())
                                    call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3523")
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func001Func004C() ) then
                                        call SetUnitManaBJ(GetSpellTargetUnit(), 0)
                                        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rag1', GetTriggerUnit())
                                        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3526")
                                    else
                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3525")
                                    endif
                                endif
                            else
                                // Mining
                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003C() ) then
                                    set udg_TempPoint=GetDestructableLoc(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                                    call KillDestructable(GetSpellTargetDestructable())
                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func006C() ) then
                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func006Func002C() ) then
                                            call CreateItemLoc('sor8', udg_TempPoint)
                                            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 7 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3417")
                                        else
                                            call CreateItemLoc('sorf', udg_TempPoint)
                                            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 5 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3414")
                                        endif
                                        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func006Func001C() ) then
                                            call CreateItemLoc('sor9', udg_TempPoint)
                                            call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                            call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 5 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3415")
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func006Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                call CreateItemLoc('sorf', udg_TempPoint)
                                                call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
                                                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( 5 + ( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3416")
                                            else
                                                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) * 3 ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                else
                                    // Gravestones
                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003C() ) then
                                        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 9)
                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004C() ) then
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3498")
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001C() ) then
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3497")
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3496")
                                                else
                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3495")
                                                    else
                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3494")
                                                        else
                                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3493")
                                                            else
                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3492")
                                                                else
                                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func004Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3491")
                                                                    else
                                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3490")
                                                                    endif
                                                                endif
                                                            endif
                                                        endif
                                                    endif
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    else
                                        // Info
                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002C() ) then
                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3438")
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3439")
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3463")
                                                else
                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3437")
                                                        else
                                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                                call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetSpellTargetDestructable(), "stand")
                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                                    set udg_TempItem=GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'sora')
                                                                    set udg_TempInt=GetItemCharges(udg_TempItem)
                                                                else
                                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                                        set udg_TempItem=GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'wcyc')
                                                                        set udg_TempInt=GetItemCharges(udg_TempItem)
                                                                    else
                                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                            set udg_TempItem=GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'tmmt')
                                                                            set udg_TempInt=( GetItemCharges(udg_TempItem) * 2 )
                                                                        else
                                                                            set udg_TempItem=GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'shcw')
                                                                            set udg_TempInt=( GetItemCharges(udg_TempItem) * 2 )
                                                                        endif
                                                                    endif
                                                                endif
                                                                call RemoveItem(udg_TempItem)
                                                                call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('shrs', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                                call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), udg_TempInt)
                                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3518")
                                                                call AddHeroXPSwapped(( GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit()) + ( udg_TempInt * 2 ) ), GetTriggerUnit(), true)
                                                            else
                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func009C() ) then
                                                                    call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(- 10, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
                                                                    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('cosl', GetTriggerUnit())
                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3566")
                                                                else
                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3442")
                                                                endif
                                                            endif
                                                        endif
                                                    else
                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3440")
                                                        else
                                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                                call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3441")
                                                            else
                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3435")
                                                                else
                                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3436")
                                                                    else
                                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3462")
                                                                        else
                                                                            // Signs
                                                                            if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
                                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
                                                                                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Moladune)
                                                                                    set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Gib_Town)
                                                                                    call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempLoc, 2.00)
                                                                                    call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3500")
                                                                                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
                                                                                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                                                else
                                                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                                                        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Moladune)
                                                                                        set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Sanctuary)
                                                                                        call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempLoc, 2.00)
                                                                                        call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                                                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3501")
                                                                                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
                                                                                        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                                                    else
                                                                                        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                                            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Ashwell)
                                                                                            set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Sanctuary)
                                                                                            call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempLoc, 2.00)
                                                                                            call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                                                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3502")
                                                                                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
                                                                                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                                                        else
                                                                                            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Sanctuary)
                                                                                            set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Discover_Gib_Town)
                                                                                            call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempLoc, 2.00)
                                                                                            call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
                                                                                            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3503")
                                                                                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
                                                                                            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                                                                                        endif
                                                                                    endif
                                                                                endif
                                                                            else
                                                                                if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                                                                                    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3543")
                                                                                else
                                                                                    if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func004Func001Func004Func001Func002Func001Func003Func003Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001Func001Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                                                        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetSpellTargetUnit(), "attack", GetTriggerUnit())
                                                                                        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_3796")
                                                                                    else
                                                                                    endif
                                                                                endif
                                                                            endif
                                                                        endif
                                                                    endif
                                                                endif
                                                            endif
                                                        endif
                                                    endif
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Interact_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()
            // Logging
            call EnumDestructablesInCircleBJ(75.00, udg_TempPoint, function Trig_Interact_Func002Func001Func004A)
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        else
        endif
    endif
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Interact takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Interact=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Interact, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Interact, Condition(function Trig_Interact_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Interact, function Trig_Interact_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Ashwell Reveal
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Ashwell_Reveal_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_VisitedAshwell[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ashwell_Reveal_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_ntav_0008)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncop', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_MapPing, 100, udg_TempPoint, 0)
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_2650")
    call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    set udg_VisitedAshwell[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Ashwell_Reveal takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Ashwell_Reveal=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Ashwell_Reveal, gg_rct_Discover_Ashwell)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Ashwell_Reveal, Condition(function Trig_Ashwell_Reveal_Conditions))

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Gib Town Reveal
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Gib_Town_Reveal_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerInForce(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_NeutralPlayers) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_VisitedGibTown[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Gib_Town_Reveal_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_ntav_0019)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ncop', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call PlaySoundAtPointBJ(gg_snd_MapPing, 100, udg_TempPoint, 0)
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_2748")
    call PingMinimapLocForForce(udg_TempForce, udg_TempPoint, 2.00)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    set udg_VisitedGibTown[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
endfunction

    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Gib_Town_Reveal, Condition(function Trig_Gib_Town_Reveal_Conditions))

    if ( Trig_Bandit_Fort_Gate_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_BanditGateOpen=false
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_CLOSE, gg_dest_DTg3_5552)
    else
        set udg_BanditGateOpen=true
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_DTg3_5552)
    endif
    call TriggerSleepAction(30.00)

endfunction

    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Ship to Ashwell
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetSoldItem()) == 'k3m1' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func007C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetBuyingUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Shipyard_Start)
    else
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Moladune_Shipyard_Start)
    endif
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00N', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, ( GetUnitFacing(GetBuyingUnit()) + 180.00 ))
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(100.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "creepdevour", GetBuyingUnit())
    set udg_TempUnit=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func007C() ) then
        call SetCameraTargetControllerNoZForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), GetLastCreatedUnit(), 0, 0, false)
    else
    endif
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.20)
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Func009C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ocean_2)
    else
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Waterfall_11)
    endif
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_TempUnit, "move", udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Ship_to_Ashwell takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Ship_to_Ashwell=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Ship_to_Ashwell, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SELL_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Ship_to_Ashwell, Condition(function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Ship_to_Ashwell, function Trig_Ship_to_Ashwell_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Ship to Moladune
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetSoldItem()) == 'kybl' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetBuyingUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'nshp' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Shipyard_Start)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00M', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, ( GetUnitFacing(GetBuyingUnit()) + 180.00 ))
    else
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ashwell_Shipyard_Start)
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'n00N', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, ( GetUnitFacing(GetBuyingUnit()) + 180.00 ))
    endif
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(100.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "creepdevour", GetBuyingUnit())
    set udg_TempUnit=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func006C() ) then
        call SetCameraTargetControllerNoZForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()), GetLastCreatedUnit(), 0, 0, false)
    else
    endif
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.20)
    if ( Trig_Ship_to_Moladune_Func008C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Bridge_21)
    else
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ocean_1)
    endif
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(udg_TempUnit, "move", udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Ship_to_Moladune, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SELL_ITEM)

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Ashwell End
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Ashwell_End_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00N' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ashwell_End_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_DestroyedAshwell == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ashwell_End_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "unloadall", udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    if ( Trig_Ashwell_End_Func005C() ) then
        call RemoveUnit(GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        call KillUnit(GetTriggerUnit())
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================

    set gg_trg_Ashwell_End=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Ashwell_End, gg_rct_Ashwell_Shipyard)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Ashwell_End, Condition(function Trig_Ashwell_End_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Ashwell_End, function Trig_Ashwell_End_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Bridge_1_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00M' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00N' ) ) then
        return true
    endif

        return false
    endif
    return true

    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00M' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Bridge_1_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Bridge_12)
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\MassTeleport\\MassTeleportTarget.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    if ( Trig_Bridge_1_Func007C() ) then
        set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Sanctuary_Shipyard)
    else
        set udg_TempLoc=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ocean_2)
    endif
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "move", udg_TempLoc)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Bridge_1=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Bridge_1, gg_rct_Bridge_11)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Bridge_1, Condition(function Trig_Bridge_1_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Bridge_1, function Trig_Bridge_1_Actions)
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Hardmode == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitInvulnerable(GetTriggerUnit(), false)
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04F', GetTriggerUnit())
    if ( Trig_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable_Func004C() ) then
        call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A04F', GetTriggerUnit(), 2)
    else
    endif
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_GraveyardGroup)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable=CreateTrigger()

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable, function Trig_Rescued_Units_Vulnerable_Actions)
endfunction

    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'U007' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'U00A' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Necromancer_AI_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Necromancer_AI_Func005C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ArmyOfDead == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    set udg_ArmyOfDead=true
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "darkportal", udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call TriggerSleepAction(90.00)
    set udg_ArmyOfDead=false
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Necromancer Respawn
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == udg_Necromancer ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(udg_Necromancer) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002Func001C() ) then
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_GraveyardGroup)
    else
        if ( Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
            call RemoveLocation(udg_DeathPoint)
            set udg_DeathPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())
            call ReviveHeroLoc(udg_Necromancer, udg_DeathPoint, true)
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call TriggerSleepAction(60.00)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GraveyardGroup, function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Func002A)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Necromancer_Respawn takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Necromancer_Respawn=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Necromancer_Respawn, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Necromancer_Respawn, Condition(function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Necromancer_Respawn, function Trig_Necromancer_Respawn_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Zombie AI
//
// Victory check here.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Zombie_AI_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Victory == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ZombieCount <= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Victory == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func002002002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func002002002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsPlayerEnemy(GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()), Player(11)) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func002002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanAnd((IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true), (IsPlayerEnemy(GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()), Player(11)) == true)) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 15 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 24 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Hardmode == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 5 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 10 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 15 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 20 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 24 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( udg_SpecialCount == 30 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_SpecialCount == ( udg_SpecialLimit / 2 ) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_SpecialCount == udg_SpecialLimit ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func007Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitCurrentOrder(GetEnumUnit()) != String2OrderIdBJ("move") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func007A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func007Func001C() ) then
        call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetEnumUnit(), "attack", udg_TempPoint)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func009Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempLoc=GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())
    call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_TempLoc, 3.00)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ZombieRadar == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_ZombieCount <= 10 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Victory == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_AI_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func005C() ) then
        call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Victory)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006C() ) then
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func002002002))
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GroupPickRandomUnit(udg_TempGroup))
         call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
        if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, udg_SpecialZombie[8], Player(11), udg_DeathPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            set udg_SpecialCount=0
        else
            if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001C() ) then
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, udg_SpecialZombie[GetRandomInt(6, 7)], Player(11), udg_DeathPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
            else
                if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, udg_SpecialZombie[GetRandomInt(1, 5)], Player(11), udg_DeathPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func005Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, udg_SpecialZombie[GetRandomInt(6, 8)], Player(11), udg_DeathPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
        set udg_SpecialCount=( udg_SpecialCount + 1 )
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_ZombieGroup, function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func007A)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        if ( Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func009C() ) then
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_ZombieGroup, function Trig_Zombie_AI_Func006Func009Func001A)
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Zombie_AI takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Zombie_AI=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Zombie_AI)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Zombie_AI, 60.00)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Zombie_AI, Condition(function Trig_Zombie_AI_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Zombie_AI, function Trig_Zombie_AI_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Zombie Spawn Control
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) == Player(11) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A04F', GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Hardmode == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04F', GetEnumUnit())
    if ( Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
        call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A04F', GetEnumUnit(), 2)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ZombieCount < 100 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ZombieCount > 200 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_ZombieGroup)
    set udg_ZombieCount=( udg_ZombieCount + 1 )
    if ( Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003C() ) then
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GraveyardGroup, function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func001A)
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A03S', Player(11))
    else
        if ( Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002C() ) then
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_GraveyardGroup, function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Func003Func002Func001A)
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(true, 'A03S', Player(11))
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Zombie_Spawn_Control takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Zombie_Spawn_Control=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Zombie_Spawn_Control, GetPlayableMapRect())
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Zombie_Spawn_Control, Condition(function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Zombie_Spawn_Control, function Trig_Zombie_Spawn_Control_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Summoned AI
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Summoned_AI_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_HeroSummons[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_HeroSummonGroup[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]) > 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOrderTargetUnit() != null ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("attack") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOrderTargetUnit() != null ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitEnemy(GetOrderTargetUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOrderTargetUnit() != null ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("smart") ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("move") ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("patrol") ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summoned_AI_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    set udg_SummonedInt=GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004C() ) then
        call GroupTargetOrderBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "move", udg_PlayerHero[udg_SummonedInt])
    else
        if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
                call GroupTargetOrderBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "attack", GetOrderTargetUnit())
            else
                if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
                    call GroupTargetOrderBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "move", udg_PlayerHero[udg_SummonedInt])
                else
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetOrderPointLoc()
                    call GroupPointOrderLocBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "attack", udg_TempPoint)
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                endif
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Summoned_AI_Func004Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call GroupTargetOrderBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "attack", GetOrderTargetUnit())
                else
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetOrderPointLoc()
                    call GroupPointOrderLocBJ(udg_HeroSummonGroup[udg_SummonedInt], "attack", udg_TempPoint)
                    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
                endif
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Summoned_AI takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Summoned_AI=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Summoned_AI, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Summoned_AI, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_POINT_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Summoned_AI, Condition(function Trig_Summoned_AI_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Summoned_AI, function Trig_Summoned_AI_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func014C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00K' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n003' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00G' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00J' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n012' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00I' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00M' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o00A' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) == Player(8) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func014C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_MilitiaRepawn == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002Func002Func001Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00K' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n003' ) ) then
        return true
    endif

endfunction

    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(gg_unit_e004_0138) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002Func002Func001Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(gg_unit_o00B_0086) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o00A' ) ) then
        return false
    endif

    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00M' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(gg_unit_h00Q_0089) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00G' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h00J' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n012' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(gg_unit_h00Q_0087) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_MilitiaRepawn=false
    if ( Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Human)
    else
        if ( Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002C() ) then
            set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Dwarf)
        else
            if ( Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Orc)
            else
                if ( Trig_Militia_Respawn_Func002Func002Func002Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_TempPoint=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Barracks_Elf)
                else
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    set udg_TempLoc=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()), Player(8), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call RemoveGuardPosition(GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\Heal\\HealTarget.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "attack", udg_TempLoc)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
    set udg_MilitiaRepawn=true
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Militia_Respawn takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Militia_Respawn=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Militia_Respawn, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Militia_Respawn, Condition(function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Militia_Respawn, function Trig_Militia_Respawn_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Give Units
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Give_Units_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsPlayerAlly(ConvertedPlayer(S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, 7))), GetTriggerPlayer()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(ConvertedPlayer(S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, 7)))) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(ConvertedPlayer(S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, 7)))) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Give_Units_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()) == GetTriggerPlayer() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Give_Units_Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Give_Units_Func004Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt), true)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Give_Units_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]=true
    set udg_TempInt=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, 7))
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsSelectedAll(GetTriggerPlayer())
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Give_Units_Func004A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer())
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, ( "You gave some units to " + ( udg_PlayerColor[udg_TempInt] + ( GetPlayerName(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt)) + "|r." ) ) ))
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(ConvertedPlayer(udg_TempInt))
    call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r gave you some units." ) ))
    call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Give_Units takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Give_Units=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(0), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(1), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(2), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(3), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(4), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(5), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(6), "-give", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Give_Units, Player(7), "-give", true)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Give_Units, Condition(function Trig_Give_Units_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Give_Units, function Trig_Give_Units_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Suicide
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Suicide_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]=true
    call DialogClearBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog)
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2598")
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2599")
    set udg_No_Suicide=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2600")
    set udg_Yes_Suicide=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_Suicide_Dialog, GetTriggerPlayer())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Suicide takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Suicide=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(0), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(1), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(2), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(3), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(4), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(5), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(6), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Suicide, Player(7), "-suicide", true)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Suicide, Condition(function Trig_Suicide_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Suicide, function Trig_Suicide_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Zoom
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Zoom_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zoom_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, StringLength(GetEventPlayerChatString())) == "" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zoom_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempReal < 500.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zoom_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempReal > 4000.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zoom_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_AntiSpam[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]=true
    if ( Trig_Zoom_Func002C() ) then
        return
    else
    endif
    set udg_TempReal=S2R(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, StringLength(GetEventPlayerChatString())))
    if ( Trig_Zoom_Func004C() ) then
        call SetCameraFieldForPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer(), CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 4000.00, 0.20)
        set udg_TempReal=4000.00
        set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer())
        call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_2595")
        call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
    else
        if ( Trig_Zoom_Func004Func001C() ) then
            call SetCameraFieldForPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer(), CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 500.00, 0.20)
            set udg_TempReal=500.00
            set udg_TempForce=GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer())
            call DisplayTextToForce(udg_TempForce, "TRIGSTR_2594")
            call DestroyForce(udg_TempForce)
        else
            call SetCameraFieldForPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer(), CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, udg_TempReal, 0.20)
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Zoom takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Zoom=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(0), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(1), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(2), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(3), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(4), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(5), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(6), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Zoom, Player(7), "-zoom", false)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Zoom, Condition(function Trig_Zoom_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Zoom, function Trig_Zoom_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Item Cleanup
//
// Original mechanics by Trilititi, made portable for GUI users by Bribe.
// Disclaimer: Don't set the life of a dead item unless you know what you are doing.
// It will bug the system if you set a dead item's life to a value between 0 and 1.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func010Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemLifeBJ(GetEnumItem()) == 0.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func010A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func010Func001C() ) then
        set udg_ItemsToClean=( udg_ItemsToClean + 1 )
        set udg_CleanedItem[udg_ItemsToClean]=GetEnumItem()
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func011C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ItemsToClean >= 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ItemCleanupFlag == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_ItemCleanupFlag=false
        //  
        // Loop through all dead items and remove them
        //  
        set udg_Loop=0
        loop
            exitwhen udg_Loop > udg_ItemsToClean
            call SetItemLifeBJ(udg_CleanedItem[udg_Loop], 1.00)
            call RemoveItem(udg_CleanedItem[udg_Loop])
            set udg_CleanedItem[udg_Loop]=null
            set udg_Loop=udg_Loop + 1
        endloop
    else
        //  
        // Clean up all dead items on the map every 15 seconds
        //  
        set udg_ItemsToClean=- 1
        call EnumItemsInRectBJ(GetPlayableMapRect(), function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func010A)
        if ( Trig_Item_Cleanup_Func001Func011C() ) then
            //  
            // Start a 1.50 second timer to give time for any death animations to play
            //  
            call StartTimerBJ(udg_ItemCleanupTimer, false, 1.50)
            set udg_ItemCleanupFlag=true
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Item_Cleanup takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Item_Cleanup=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Item_Cleanup)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Item_Cleanup, 15.00)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerExpireEventBJ(gg_trg_Item_Cleanup, udg_ItemCleanupTimer)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Item_Cleanup, function Trig_Item_Cleanup_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Add Charges
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Add_Charges_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemType(GetManipulatedItem()) == ITEM_TYPE_CHARGED ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Add_Charges_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()) != GetManipulatedItem() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Add_Charges_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Add_Charges_Func002Func001C() ) then
            call SetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()), ( GetItemCharges(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) + GetItemCharges(GetManipulatedItem()) ))
            call RemoveItem(GetManipulatedItem())
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Add_Charges takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Add_Charges=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Add_Charges, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_PICKUP_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Add_Charges, Condition(function Trig_Add_Charges_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Add_Charges, function Trig_Add_Charges_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Split Charges
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Split_Charges_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_OrderID >= 852002 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_OrderID <= 852007 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOrderTargetItem() == UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetOrderedUnit(), ( udg_OrderID - 852001 )) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetItemCharges(GetOrderTargetItem()) > 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Split_Charges_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_OrderID=GetIssuedOrderId()
    if ( Trig_Split_Charges_Func002C() ) then
        call SetItemCharges(GetOrderTargetItem(), ( GetItemCharges(GetOrderTargetItem()) - 1 ))
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetOrderedUnit())
        call CreateItemLoc(GetItemTypeId(GetOrderTargetItem()), udg_TempPoint)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        call SetItemUserData(GetLastCreatedItem(), 24)
        call SetItemCharges(GetLastCreatedItem(), 1)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Split_Charges takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Split_Charges=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Split_Charges, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ISSUED_TARGET_ORDER)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Split_Charges, function Trig_Split_Charges_Actions)
endfunction
