// Trigger: Claws
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Claws_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'kgal' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'gcel' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Claws_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Claws_Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'kgal') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'gcel') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claws_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == 'kgal' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claws_Func003Func007Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == udg_RecipeFactor[GetForLoopIndexB()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claws_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claws_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Claws_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempInt=( udg_TempInt + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Claws_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Ingredients=3
        set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='kgal'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='kgal'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[3]='gcel'
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Claws_Func003Func007Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ratc', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Claws=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Claws, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_PICKUP_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Claws, Condition(function Trig_Claws_Conditions))

    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'ratc' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'oven' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'amrc' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

    if ( not Trig_Assassin_Blade_Func008C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'ratc') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'oven') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'amrc') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) != 'H006' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assassin_Blade_Func006Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == udg_RecipeFactor[GetForLoopIndexB()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Assassin_Blade_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Ingredients=3
    set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='ratc'
    set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='oven'
    set udg_RecipeFactor[3]='amrc'
    set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Assassin_Blade_Func006Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('asbl', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

    set udg_RecipeFactor[3]='rlif'
    set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients

                set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('stwa', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claymore_Func003Func005Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == udg_RecipeFactor[GetForLoopIndexB()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claymore_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Claymore_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Claymore_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempInt=( udg_TempInt + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Claymore_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Ingredients=2
        set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='rat9'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='rat9'
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Claymore_Func003Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('dthb', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Claymore=CreateTrigger()

    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Glamdring_Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('srbd', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

    endif
    return true

        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Thorn_Mail_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Thorn_Mail_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Thorn_Mail_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempInt=( udg_TempInt + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Thorn_Mail_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Ingredients=3
        set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='kgal'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='kgal'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[3]='rde4'
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Thorn_Mail_Func003Func007Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('cnhn', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'rde0') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'gemt') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), 'penr') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Enchanted_Cloak_Func007Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA())) == udg_RecipeFactor[GetForLoopIndexB()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Enchanted_Cloak_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Ingredients=4
    set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='rin1'
    set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='rde0'
    set udg_RecipeFactor[3]='gemt'
    set udg_RecipeFactor[4]='penr'
    set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Enchanted_Cloak_Func007Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ciri', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Mage_Sandals_Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ratf', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Mystic_Charm_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Mystic_Charm_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempInt=( udg_TempInt + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Mystic_Charm_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Ingredients=2
        set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='amrc'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='amrc'
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Mystic_Charm_Func003Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('evtl', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Ring_of_Health_Func003Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('rnsp', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

function InitTrig_Ring_of_Health takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Ring_of_Health=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Ring_of_Health, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_PICKUP_ITEM)

    endif

    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Ring_of_the_Magi_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempInt=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Ring_of_the_Magi_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_TempInt=( udg_TempInt + 1 )
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    if ( Trig_Ring_of_the_Magi_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_Ingredients=2
        set udg_RecipeFactor[1]='gemt'
        set udg_RecipeFactor[2]='gemt'
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=false
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=6
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
            set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=udg_Ingredients
            loop
                exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
                if ( Trig_Ring_of_the_Magi_Func003Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call RemoveItem(UnitItemInSlotBJ(GetManipulatingUnit(), GetForLoopIndexA()))
                    set udg_FactorCleared[GetForLoopIndexB()]=true
                else
                endif
                set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
            endloop
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('ram4', GetTriggerUnit())
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Arrow Rain
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A02F' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitEnemy(GetEnumUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_MECHANICAL) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_TempGroup) > 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005Func001C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
            call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "cripple", GetEnumUnit())
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o000', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(300.00, udg_TempPoint)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Func005A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Arrow_Rain takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Arrow_Rain=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Arrow_Rain, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Arrow_Rain, Condition(function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Arrow_Rain, function Trig_Arrow_Rain_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Charge Finish
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Charge_Finish_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetAttacker()) == 'H00F' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(GetAttacker(), 'Bspe') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Charge_Finish_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempReal=( 50.00 + ( 50.00 * I2R(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A03K', GetAttacker())) ) )
    call UnitDamageTargetBJ(GetAttacker(), GetTriggerUnit(), udg_TempReal, ATTACK_TYPE_MELEE, DAMAGE_TYPE_FIRE)
    call UnitRemoveBuffBJ('Bspe', GetAttacker())
    call SetUnitPathing(GetAttacker(), true)
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A03L', GetAttacker())
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetAttacker())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o000', GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "thunderbolt", GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(2.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call CreateTextTagLocBJ(( ( "|cffff0000" + I2S(R2I(udg_TempReal)) ) + "!" ), udg_TempPoint, 0, 10, 100, 0.00, 0.00, 0)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempFloatText=GetLastCreatedTextTag()
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Floating_Text_Fadeout)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Charge_Finish takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Charge_Finish=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Charge_Finish, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Charge_Finish, Condition(function Trig_Charge_Finish_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Charge_Finish, function Trig_Charge_Finish_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Charge Start
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Charge_Start_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A03K' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Charge_Start_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitPathing(GetTriggerUnit(), false)
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A03L', GetTriggerUnit())
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_TrampleGroup)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Charge_Start takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Charge_Start=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Charge_Start, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Charge_Start, Condition(function Trig_Charge_Start_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Charge_Start, function Trig_Charge_Start_Actions)

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Command
//
// This contains triggers for logging, mining and gathering.
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Command_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04H' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func002002003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()) == Player(11) )
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func002002003002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == false )
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func002002003 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanAnd((GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()) == Player(11)), (IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == false)) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func003Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( IsDestructableAliveBJ(GetSpellTargetDestructable()) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetSpellTargetUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Command_Func003Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Func004Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocMatching(700.00, udg_TempPoint, Condition(function Trig_Command_Func002002003))
    if ( Trig_Command_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_TempLoc=GetUnitLoc(GetSpellTargetUnit())
    else
        set udg_TempLoc=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    endif
    call GroupPointOrderLocBJ(udg_TempGroup, "attack", udg_TempLoc)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Command takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Command=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Command, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Command, Condition(function Trig_Command_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Command, function Trig_Command_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Demolish
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Demolish_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A026' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Demolish_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetTriggerUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Demolish_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call TriggerSleepAction(2)
    if ( Trig_Demolish_Func002C() ) then
        call KillUnit(GetTriggerUnit())
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(20, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(30, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Demolish takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Demolish=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Demolish, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Demolish, Condition(function Trig_Demolish_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Demolish, function Trig_Demolish_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Drunk Effects
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'rej2' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'pclr' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Drunk_Effects_Func006C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'BNdh') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o000', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(1.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    if ( Trig_Drunk_Effects_Func004C() ) then
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "sleep", GetTriggerUnit())
    else
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "drunkenhaze", GetTriggerUnit())
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Drunk_Effects takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Drunk_Effects=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Drunk_Effects, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_USE_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Drunk_Effects, Condition(function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Drunk_Effects, function Trig_Drunk_Effects_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Execute
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Execute_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A02V' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Execute_Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitFacing(GetSpellAbilityUnit()) >= ( GetUnitFacing(GetSpellTargetUnit()) - 75.00 ) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitFacing(GetSpellAbilityUnit()) <= ( GetUnitFacing(GetSpellTargetUnit()) + 75.00 ) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Execute_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitLifePercent(GetSpellTargetUnit()) <= 33.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Execute_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempReal=0.00
    if ( Trig_Execute_Func003C() ) then
        set udg_TempReal=GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetSpellTargetUnit())
        call KillUnit(GetSpellTargetUnit())
    else
        set udg_TempReal=( ( 50.00 * I2R(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped(GetSpellAbilityId(), GetTriggerUnit())) ) + 250.00 )
        if ( Trig_Execute_Func003Func002C() ) then
            set udg_TempReal=( udg_TempReal * 2.00 )
            call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("chest", GetSpellTargetUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Other\\Stampede\\StampedeMissileDeath.mdl")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        else
        endif
    endif
    call UnitDamageTargetBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetSpellTargetUnit(), udg_TempReal, ATTACK_TYPE_MELEE, DAMAGE_TYPE_FIRE)
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateTextTagLocBJ(( ( "|cffff0000" + I2S(R2I(udg_TempReal)) ) + "!" ), udg_TempPoint, 0, 10, 100, 0.00, 0.00, 0)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    set udg_TempFloatText=GetLastCreatedTextTag()
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Floating_Text_Fadeout)
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.65)
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "Stand Ready")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Execute takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Execute=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Execute, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Execute, Condition(function Trig_Execute_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Execute, function Trig_Execute_Actions)
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

    set udg_J_Collision=false
    set udg_J_TargetPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()

    set udg_J_Speed=15.00
    set udg_J_SpecialEffect="Abilities\\Spells\\Items\\OrbCorruption\\OrbCorruptionSpecialArt.mdl"
    set udg_J_Animation="attack"
    set udg_J_AnimationSpeed=0.60
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Jump_System)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Holy_Light_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A034' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitEnemy(GetSpellTargetUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Holy_Light_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A034', GetTriggerUnit()) >= 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Holy_Light_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A01C', GetSpellTargetUnit())
    if ( Trig_Holy_Light_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_TempReal=300.00
        call UnitDamageTargetBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), GetSpellTargetUnit(), udg_TempReal, ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL, DAMAGE_TYPE_FIRE)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Summon Bear
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'n006' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'n00C' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Summon_Bear_Func002C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func003002002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'n006' )
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func003002002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'n00C' )
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func003002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanOr((GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'n006'), (GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'n00C')) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetEnumUnit(), udg_TempPoint)
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetEnumUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\MassTeleport\\MassTeleportTarget.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_HasPet[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))] == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Summon_Bear_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_HasPet[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))]=true
    else
        call RemoveUnit(GetSummonedUnit())
        set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsOfPlayerMatching(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), Condition(function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func003002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Summon_Bear_Func001Func004A)
         call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Summon_Bear takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Summon_Bear=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Summon_Bear, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SUMMON)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Summon_Bear, Condition(function Trig_Summon_Bear_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Summon_Bear, function Trig_Summon_Bear_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Summon Bear Death

        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'n00C' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A012' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'ACfs' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'ANfs' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'S004' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Throw_Torch_Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006Func001Func005Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( LoadUnitHandleBJ(GetForLoopIndexA(), 0, udg_FireHashtable) == GetEnumUnit() ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit()) == 'n015' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitAnimation(GetEnumUnit(), "stand")
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('Avul', GetEnumUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A01F', GetEnumUnit())
        set udg_TempLoc=GetSpellTargetLoc()
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_LightCounter
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006Func001Func005Func001C() ) then
                call CreateDestructableLoc('XOk2', udg_TempLoc, bj_UNIT_FACING, 1, 0)
                call SaveDestructableHandleBJ(GetLastCreatedDestructable(), GetForLoopIndexA(), 1, udg_FireHashtable)
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempLoc)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func002Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITf1' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'ITx3' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'YT15' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT06' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'LT04' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

        return true

        return true

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Weather_Current != 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func005C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001C() ) then
        call KillDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
        if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func004C() ) then
            set udg_TempPoint=GetDestructableLoc(GetEnumDestructable())
            if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func004Func003C() ) then
                set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 3)
                if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func004Func003Func002C() ) then
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenp', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                else
                    if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func004Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nepl', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    else
                        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nenc', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
                    endif
                endif
            else
                call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'e006', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
            endif
            call SetUnitAnimation(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "birth")
            call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetLastCreatedUnit(), "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\NightElf\\EntBirthTarget\\EntBirthTarget.mdl")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        else
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func002C() ) then
            call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), "stand")
        else
            if ( Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008Func001Func002Func003C() ) then
                set udg_TempPoint=GetDestructableLoc(GetEnumDestructable())
                call RemoveDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
                call CreateDestructableLoc('ITx3', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1.10, 0)
                call SetDestructableInvulnerableBJ(GetLastCreatedDestructable(), true)
                call CreateDestructableLoc('XOk2', udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1.00, 0)
                call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Throw_Torch_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o008', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), udg_TempPoint, GetRandomDirectionDeg())
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    set udg_TempGroup=GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(200.00, udg_TempPoint)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_TempGroup, function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func006A)
     call DestroyGroup(udg_TempGroup)
    call EnumDestructablesInCircleBJ(200.00, udg_TempPoint, function Trig_Throw_Torch_Func008A)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Throw_Torch takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Throw_Torch=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Throw_Torch, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Throw_Torch, Condition(function Trig_Throw_Torch_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Throw_Torch, function Trig_Throw_Torch_Actions)
endfunction

        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Avul', GetEnumUnit())
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=1
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=udg_LightCounter

            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Throw_Water_Func003Func001Func004Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveDestructable(LoadDestructableHandleBJ(GetForLoopIndexA(), 1, udg_FireHashtable))
            else
            endif
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop

function Trig_Throw_Water_Func005A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Throw_Water_Func005Func001C() ) then
        call DestructableRestoreLife(GetEnumDestructable(), GetDestructableMaxLife(GetEnumDestructable()), true)
    else
        if ( Trig_Throw_Water_Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
            call SetDestructableAnimationBJ(GetEnumDestructable(), "death")
        else
            if ( Trig_Throw_Water_Func005Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call RemoveDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
            else
            endif
        endif
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Zealous
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Zealous_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetAttacker()) == 'H006' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A02P', GetAttacker()) > 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetUnitManaPercent(GetAttacker()) < 100.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitEnemy(GetTriggerUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Zealous_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetAttacker(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetAttacker()) + ( 1 + I2R(GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A02P', GetAttacker())) ) ))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Zealous takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Zealous=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Zealous, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Zealous, Condition(function Trig_Zealous_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Zealous, function Trig_Zealous_Actions)
endfunction

    call SetTextTagVelocityBJ(udg_TempFloatText, 64, 90)
    call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(udg_TempFloatText, false)
    call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(udg_TempFloatText, 1.50)
    call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(udg_TempFloatText, 1.00)
endfunction

        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'wneu' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Animations_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Item_Animations_Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Item_Animations_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "attack")
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.50)
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "stand ready")
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Item_Animations takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Item_Animations=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Item_Animations, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_USE_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Item_Animations, Condition(function Trig_Item_Animations_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Item_Animations, function Trig_Item_Animations_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Jump System
//
// By: Paladon
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Jump_System_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_J_Integers[1] == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_System_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Jump_System_Func001C() ) then
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Jump_Loop)
    else
    endif
    set udg_J_Integers[1]=( udg_J_Integers[1] + 1 )
    set udg_J_Integers[2]=( udg_J_Integers[2] + 1 )
    set udg_J_TempPoint[1]=GetUnitLoc(udg_JCast_Unit)
    set udg_J_Distances[udg_J_Integers[2]]=DistanceBetweenPoints(udg_J_TempPoint[1], udg_J_TargetPoint)
    set udg_J_ReachedDistance[udg_J_Integers[2]]=0.00
    set udg_J_UnitSpeed[udg_J_Integers[2]]=udg_J_Speed
    set udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[2]]=udg_JCast_Unit
    set udg_J_Angle[udg_J_Integers[2]]=AngleBetweenPoints(udg_J_TempPoint[1], udg_J_TargetPoint)
    set udg_J_Effect[udg_J_Integers[2]]=udg_J_SpecialEffect
    set udg_J_Animations[udg_J_Integers[2]]=udg_J_Animation
    set udg_J_HeightSettings[udg_J_Integers[2]]=( udg_J_JumpHigh_Distance * udg_J_Distances[udg_J_Integers[2]] )
    call SetUnitPathing(udg_JCast_Unit, false)
    call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(udg_JCast_Unit, ( udg_J_AnimationSpeed * 100.00 ))
    call SetUnitAnimation(udg_JCast_Unit, udg_J_Animation)
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(udg_JCast_Unit, udg_J_Group)
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('Arav', udg_JCast_Unit)
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('Arav', udg_JCast_Unit)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_J_TempPoint[1])
    call RemoveLocation(udg_J_TargetPoint)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Jump_System takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Jump_System=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Jump_System, function Trig_Jump_System_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Jump Loop
//
// By: Paladon
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]]) == 'E003' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func009C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_J_Integers[1] == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func014C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetRandomInt(1, 5) == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_J_ReachedDistance[udg_J_Integers[3]] < udg_J_Distances[udg_J_Integers[3]] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInGroup(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_Group) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Jump_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_J_Integers[3]=1
    loop
        exitwhen udg_J_Integers[3] > udg_J_Integers[2]
        if ( Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call QueueUnitAnimationBJ(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_Animations[udg_J_Integers[3]])
                set udg_J_TempPoint[1]=GetUnitLoc(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]])
                set udg_J_TempPoint[2]=PolarProjectionBJ(udg_J_TempPoint[1], udg_J_UnitSpeed[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_Angle[udg_J_Integers[3]])
                call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_TempPoint[2])
                set udg_J_ReachedDistance[udg_J_Integers[3]]=( udg_J_ReachedDistance[udg_J_Integers[3]] + udg_J_UnitSpeed[udg_J_Integers[3]] )
                if ( Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func014C() ) then
                    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("chest", udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_Effect[udg_J_Integers[3]])
                    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
                else
                endif
                set udg_J_RealTimer[udg_J_Integers[3]]=( udg_J_RealTimer[udg_J_Integers[3]] + ( 180.00 / ( udg_J_Distances[udg_J_Integers[3]] / udg_J_UnitSpeed[udg_J_Integers[3]] ) ) )
                set udg_J_JumpHigh[udg_J_Integers[3]]=( SinBJ(udg_J_RealTimer[udg_J_Integers[3]]) * udg_J_HeightSettings[udg_J_Integers[3]] )
                call SetUnitFlyHeightBJ(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_JumpHigh[udg_J_Integers[3]], 1000000000.00)
                call RemoveLocation(udg_J_TempPoint[1])
                call RemoveLocation(udg_J_TempPoint[2])
            else
                call SetUnitPathing(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], true)
                call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], udg_J_Group)
                call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]], 100.00)
                call ResetUnitAnimation(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]])
                set udg_J_RealTimer[udg_J_Integers[3]]=0.00
                set udg_J_Integers[1]=( udg_J_Integers[1] - 1 )
                if ( Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func008C() ) then
                    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'o000', GetOwningPlayer(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]]), GetUnitLoc(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]]), bj_UNIT_FACING)
                    call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A03B', GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A03A', udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]]))
                    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
                    call IssueImmediateOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "creepthunderclap")
                    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_J_Unit[udg_J_Integers[3]]), "Abilities\\Spells\\Orc\\WarStomp\\WarStompCaster.mdl")
                    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
                else
                endif
                if ( Trig_Jump_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func009C() ) then
                    set udg_J_Integers[2]=0
                    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
                else
                endif
            endif
        else
        endif
        set udg_J_Integers[3]=udg_J_Integers[3] + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Jump_Loop takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Jump_Loop=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Jump_Loop)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Jump_Loop, 0.02)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Jump_Loop, function Trig_Jump_Loop_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_ON_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'hrdh' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( IsUnitType(GetTriggerUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_HERO) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

    if ( not ( GetIssuedOrderIdBJ() == String2OrderIdBJ("replenishon") ) ) then
        return false
    endif

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_Backpack_Group)
    if ( Trig_Pick_up_Items_ON_Func004C() ) then
        call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Pick_up_Items_Loop)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Pick up Items Loop
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEnumItem() == null ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func001C() ) then
    else
        call IssueTargetItemOrder(GetEnumUnit(), "smart", GetEnumItem())
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(GetEnumUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_Backpack_Group)
    else
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit())
        set udg_TempRegion=RectFromCenterSizeBJ(udg_TempPoint, 1000.00, 1000.00)
        call EnumItemsInRectBJ(udg_TempRegion, function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001Func001Func003A)
        call RemoveRect(udg_TempRegion)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(udg_Backpack_Group) == 0 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    else
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_Backpack_Group, function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Func001Func001A)
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Pick_up_Items_Loop=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Pick_up_Items_Loop)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Pick_up_Items_Loop, 0.75)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Pick_up_Items_Loop, function Trig_Pick_up_Items_Loop_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Drop_Items_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00G' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Drop_Items_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopBIndex=1
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd=6
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(GetForLoopIndexB(), GetTriggerUnit())
        set bj_forLoopBIndex=bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Suicide_Dialog_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A018' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Dialog_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DialogClearBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog)
    call DialogSetMessageBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2598")
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2599")
    set udg_No_Suicide=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_Suicide_Dialog, "TRIGSTR_2600")
    set udg_Yes_Suicide=GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_Suicide_Dialog, GetTriggerPlayer())
endfunction

    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Suicide_Dialog, Condition(function Trig_Suicide_Dialog_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Suicide_Dialog, function Trig_Suicide_Dialog_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Suicide Yes
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetClickedButtonBJ() == udg_Yes_Suicide ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 3 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_TempInt == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func013C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitDeadBJ(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]) == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())]) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call PauseUnitBJ(true, udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
    call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
    if ( Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003C() ) then
        call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], true)
        set udg_TempInt=GetRandomInt(1, 4)
        if ( Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r" ) ) + " commited suicide." ))
        else
            if ( Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003Func001C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r" ) ) + " offed himself." ))
            else
                if ( Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func003Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r" ) ) + " ended his misery." ))
                else
                    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( ( udg_PlayerColor[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "|r" ) ) + " did a harakiri." ))
                endif
            endif
        endif
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
        set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_TempPoint, "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\Human\\HumanLargeDeathExplode\\HumanLargeDeathExplode.mdl")
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
        call PauseUnitBJ(false, udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
        call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())], false)
        call KillUnit(udg_PlayerHero[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())])
        call TriggerSleepAction(6.00)
        if ( Trig_Suicide_Yes_Func003Func013C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_2601")
            call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_SuicideTaunt)
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Suicide_Yes=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterDialogEventBJ(gg_trg_Suicide_Yes, udg_Suicide_Dialog)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Suicide_Yes, Condition(function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Suicide_Yes, function Trig_Suicide_Yes_Actions)
endfunction

    call DestroyEffectBJ(udg_SpecialFX)
endfunction

endfunction

function RunInitializationTriggers takes nothing returns nothing
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Initialization)
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Timer_On)
endfunction

//***************************************************************************

//*  Main Initialization
//*
//***************************************************************************

//===========================================================================
function main takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetCameraBounds(- 15616.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), - 13824.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM), 15616.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), 13312.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), - 15616.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), 13312.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), 15616.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), - 13824.0 + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM))
    call SetDayNightModels("Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronTerrain\\DNCLordaeronTerrain.mdl", "Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronUnit\\DNCLordaeronUnit.mdl")
    call SetWaterBaseColor(128, 128, 128, 255)
    call NewSoundEnvironment("Default")
    call SetAmbientDaySound("VillageDay")
    call SetAmbientNightSound("VillageNight")
    call SetMapMusic("Music", true, 0)
    call InitSounds()
    call CreateRegions()
    call CreateAllDestructables()
    call CreateAllUnits()
    call InitBlizzard()


    call InitGlobals()
    call InitCustomTriggers()
    call RunInitializationTriggers()

endfunction

//***************************************************************************
//*
//*  Map Configuration
//*
//***************************************************************************

function config takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetMapName("TRIGSTR_001")
    call SetMapDescription("TRIGSTR_003")
    call SetPlayers(11)
    call SetTeams(11)
    call SetGamePlacement(MAP_PLACEMENT_TEAMS_TOGETHER)

    call DefineStartLocation(0, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(1, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(2, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(3, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(4, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(5, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(6, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(7, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(8, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(9, - 512.0, - 960.0)
    call DefineStartLocation(10, - 512.0, - 960.0)

    // Player setup
    call InitCustomPlayerSlots()
    call InitCustomTeams()
    call InitAllyPriorities()
endfunction
